+_SENSORY_SEED_FACETS: Tuple[Tuple[str, str], ...] = (
+    ("audio", "tone"),
+    ("audio", "timbre"),
+    ("audio", "rhythm"),
+    ("visual", "hue"),

+def _sensory_crystal_needs_seeding(state_dir: str) -> bool:
+    try:
+        import gzip
+
+        base = Path(state_dir) / "sensory_crystal"
+        concept_nodes = 0
+        checked = 0
+        for domain, facet in _SENSORY_SEED_FACETS:
+            path = base / domain / facet / "state.agb"
+            if not path.exists():
+                return True
+            with gzip.open(path, "rb") as fh:
+                data = json.loads(fh.read())
+            nodes = data.get("nodes", {}) if isinstance(data, dict) else {}
+            concept_nodes += sum(
+                1
+                for value in nodes.values()
+                if isinstance(value, dict) and value.get("stage") == "concept"
+            )
+            checked += 1
+
+        sem_path = base / "semantic" / "state.agb"
+        if not sem_path.exists():
+            return True
+        with gzip.open(sem_path, "rb") as fh:
+            sem_data = json.loads(fh.read())
+        semantic_nodes = sem_data.get("semantic", {}) if isinstance(sem_data, dict) else {}
+        concept_nodes += sum(
+            1
+            for value in semantic_nodes.values()
+            if isinstance(value, dict) and value.get("stage") == "concept"
+        )
+        return checked == 0 or concept_nodes == 0
+    except Exception:
+        return True
+
+
+def _ensure_seeded_sensory_crystal_state(state_dir: str, *, verbose: bool = False) -> bool:
+    if not _sensory_crystal_needs_seeding(state_dir):
+        return False
+
+    script_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "seed_sensory_crystals.py"
+    env = os.environ.copy()
+    env["AURORA_SENSORY_STATE_DIR"] = str(Path(state_dir).resolve())
+
+    try:
+        result = subprocess.run(
+            [sys.executable, str(script_path)],
+            cwd=str(script_path.parent),
+            env=env,
+            capture_output=True,
+            text=True,
+            timeout=120,
+            check=True,
+        )
+        if verbose:
+            summary = ""
+            for line in reversed((result.stdout or "").splitlines()):
+                if line.strip():
+                    summary = line.strip()
+                    break
+            print("  [SENSORY-CRYSTAL] Applied concept seed bootstrap"
+                  + (f" ({summary})" if summary else ""))
+        return True
+    except Exception as exc:
+        if verbose:
+            print(f"  [SENSORY-CRYSTAL] Seed bootstrap unavailable: {exc}")
+        return False

         profile = meaning_profile_for_signature(value)
         return dict(profile or {}) if profile else {}

+def _normalize_runtime_profile(runtime_profile: str) -> str:
+    profile = str(runtime_profile or "full").strip().lower()
+    if profile not in {"full", "surface", "subsurface"}:
+        return "full"
+    return profile

+    def _is_broad_surface_meta_anchor(self, term: str) -> bool:
+        normalized = self._normalize_mention(term)
+        if not normalized:
+            return False
+        if normalized in self._SURFACE_META_ANCHORS:
+            return True
+        words = [
+            word
+            for word in re.findall(r"[a-z]{3,}", normalized)
+            if word not in self._WEAK_ANCHOR_LABELS
+        ]
+        return len(words) == 1 and words[0] in self._SURFACE_META_ANCHORS
+
+    def _is_explicit_meaning_or_continuity_request(
+        self,
+        user_text: str,
+        understood: Optional[dict] = None,
+    ) -> bool:
+        text_low = str(user_text or "").lower()
+        understood = dict(understood or {})
+        if str(understood.get("query_type", "") or "") == "definition":
+            return True
+        return any(marker in text_low for marker in self._EXPLICIT_MEANING_CONTINUITY_MARKERS)
+
+    def should_suppress_surface_meta_answer(
+        self,
+        user_text: str,
+        *,
+        understood: Optional[dict] = None,
+        term: str = "",
+    ) -> bool:
+        if not self._is_broad_surface_meta_anchor(term):
+            return False
+        return not self._is_explicit_meaning_or_continuity_request(user_text, understood)

+    def answer_from_speaker_owned_facts(
+        self,
+        user_text: str,
+        understood: dict | None = None,
+        systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    ) -> str:
+        user_bucket = dict(self.stated_facts.get('user', {}) or {})
+        if not user_bucket:
+            return ""
+        if understood is None:
+            try:
+                understood = UtteranceParser().parse(user_text)
+            except Exception:
+                understood = {}
+        text_low = self._normalize_mention(user_text)
+        if not text_low:
+            return ""
+
+        best_field = ""
+        best_score = 0.0
+        text_terms = set(text_low.split())
+        for field, value in user_bucket.items():
+            field_key = self._normalize_mention(field)
+            if not field_key or field_key == 'identity_label' or not str(value or '').strip():
+                continue
+            score = 0.0
+            if f"my {field_key}" in text_low:
+                score += 1.3
+            field_terms = {
+                part for part in field_key.split()
+                if len(part) >= 3 and part not in self._WEAK_ANCHOR_LABELS
+            }
+            overlap = len(field_terms & text_terms)
+            if overlap:
+                score += overlap * 0.34
+            if field_key == 'name' and re.search(r'\b(?:my\s+name|who\s+am\s+i)\b', text_low):
+                score += 1.4
+            if score > best_score:
+                best_score = score
+                best_field = field_key
+        if not best_field or best_score < 0.68:
+            return ""
+
+        value = str(user_bucket.get(best_field, '') or '').strip()
+        if not value:
+            return ""
+        core_claim = f"I should call you {value}" if best_field == 'name' else f"your {best_field} is {value}"
+        rendered = self._render_from_comprehension_intent(
+            systems,
+            core_claim=core_claim,
+            intent_type='statement',
+            emotion_tone='precise',
+            relationship_signal='neutral',
+            certainty=min(0.95, 0.78 + best_score * 0.1),
+            supporting_concepts=[best_field, value, 'user'],
+            constraints=['recall', 'speaker_fact'],
+        )
+        return str(rendered or WorkingMemory._data_to_minimal_speech(core_claim, 'precise', 'neutral')).strip()
+
+    def answer_from_recent_utterance_recall(
+        self,
+        user_text: str,
+        understood: dict | None = None,
+        systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    ) -> str:
+        if not self.recent_user_utterances:
+            return ""
+        if understood is None:
+            try:
+                understood = UtteranceParser().parse(user_text)
+            except Exception:
+                understood = {}
+        text_low = str(user_text or '').lower()
+        current_terms = set(self._utterance_terms(user_text, understood))
+        target_terms = set(dict(self._extract_context_targets(user_text, understood) or {}).get('target_terms', []) or [])
+        best_match: Dict[str, Any] = {}
+        best_score = 0.0
+        normalized_now = self._normalize_mention(user_text)
+        for idx, item in enumerate(self.recent_user_utterances):
+            candidate = dict(item or {})
+            candidate_text = str(candidate.get('text', '') or '').strip()
+            candidate_norm = self._normalize_mention(candidate.get('normalized_text', '') or candidate_text)
+            if not candidate_text or candidate_norm == normalized_now:
+                continue
+            score = max(0.0, 1.08 - idx * 0.06)
+            terms = set(candidate.get('terms', []) or [])
+            overlap = len(current_terms & terms)
+            if overlap:
+                score += overlap * 0.2
+            if target_terms:
+                score += 0.24 * len(target_terms & terms)
+            if bool(candidate.get('is_clarification')):
+                score -= 0.12
+            if score > best_score:
+                best_score = score
+                best_match = candidate
+        if not best_match or best_score < 0.9:
+            return ""
+
+        prior_text = str(best_match.get('text', '') or '').strip()
+        if not prior_text:
+            return ""
+        core_claim = f"earlier user utterance {prior_text[:220]}"
+        rendered = self._render_from_comprehension_intent(
+            systems,
+            core_claim=core_claim,
+            intent_type='statement',
+            emotion_tone='precise',
+            relationship_signal='recognition',
+            certainty=min(0.94, max(0.82, best_score)),
+            supporting_concepts=[prior_text[:220], 'earlier', 'utterance'],
+            constraints=['recall', 'utterance'],
+        )
+        return str(rendered or WorkingMemory._data_to_minimal_speech(core_claim, 'precise', 'recognition')).strip()
+
+    def answer_from_context_carryover(
+        self,
+        user_text: str,
+        understood: dict | None = None,
+        systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    ) -> str:
+        speaker_answer = str(
+            self.answer_from_speaker_owned_facts(
+                user_text,
+                understood=understood,
+                systems=systems,
+            )
+            or ""
+        ).strip()
+        if speaker_answer:
+            return speaker_answer
+
+        text_low = str(user_text or '').lower()
+        callback_like = bool(
+            (understood or {}).get('is_callback') or
+            (understood or {}).get('is_clarification') or
+            any(marker in text_low for marker in self._REFERENT_CALLBACK_MARKERS)
+        )
+        definition_callback = callback_like and any(
+            phrase in text_low for phrase in (
+                'what do you mean by',
+                'what did you mean by',
+                'what do you mean',
+                'what did you mean',
+            )
+        )
+        if definition_callback:
+            meaning_answer = str(
+                self.answer_from_meanings(
+                    user_text,
+                    understood=understood,
+                    systems=systems,
+                )
+                or ""
+            ).strip()
+            if meaning_answer:
+                return meaning_answer
+
+            semantic_frame_answer = str(
+                self.answer_from_semantic_frames(
+                    user_text,
+                    understood=understood,
+                    systems=systems,
+                )
+                or ""
+            ).strip()
+            if semantic_frame_answer:
+                return semantic_frame_answer
+
+            claim_answer = str(
+                self.answer_from_claims(
+                    user_text,
+                    understood=understood,
+                    systems=systems,
+                )
+                or ""
+            ).strip()
+            if claim_answer:
+                return claim_answer
+
+        utterance_answer = str(
+            self.answer_from_recent_utterance_recall(
+                user_text,
+                understood=understood,
+                systems=systems,
+            )
+            or ""
+        ).strip()
+        if utterance_answer:
+            return utterance_answer
+
+        try:
+            target_info = dict(self._extract_context_targets(user_text, understood) or {})
+            targets = list(target_info.get('targets', []) or [])
+        except Exception:
+            targets = []
+
+        if isinstance(systems, dict):
+            sedimemory_queries = list(dict.fromkeys(targets[:4] + ([str(user_text or '').strip()] if str(user_text or '').strip() else [])))
+            for query in sedimemory_queries:
+                recalled = _recall_semantic_sedimemory(
+                    systems,
+                    query,

+    @staticmethod
+    def _candidate_content_words(text: str) -> Set[str]:
+        stopwords = {
+            'the', 'and', 'that', 'this', 'with', 'for', 'from', 'are',
+            'was', 'can', 'may', 'its', 'also', 'such', 'some', 'any',
+            'all', 'not', 'have', 'has', 'but', 'you', 'your', 'into',
+            'onto', 'than', 'then', 'they', 'them', 'their', 'there',
+            'what', 'when', 'where', 'which', 'would', 'could', 'should',
+            'about', 'here', 'just', 'really', 'still', 'like', 'because',
+            'while', 'being', 'been', 'over', 'under', 'only', 'very',
+            'much', 'more', 'most', 'after', 'before', 'does', 'doing',
+            'did', 'through', 'across', 'between', 'people', 'person',
+        }
+        return {
+            word
+            for word in re.findall(r"[a-z]{3,}", str(text or "").lower())
+            if word not in stopwords
+        }
+
+    def _candidate_preserves_claim(
+        self,
+        candidate_text: str,
+        core_claim: str,
+        *,
+        supporting_concepts: Optional[List[str]] = None,
+    ) -> bool:
+        candidate = str(candidate_text or "").strip()
+        clean = str(core_claim or "").strip()
+        if not candidate:
+            return False
+        if candidate.lower() == clean.lower():
+            return True
+
+        claim_terms = self._candidate_content_words(clean)
+        support_terms: Set[str] = set()
+        for item in list(supporting_concepts or []):
+            support_terms.update(self._candidate_content_words(str(item or "")))
+        anchor_terms = claim_terms | support_terms
+        if not anchor_terms:
+            return True
+
+        candidate_terms = self._candidate_content_words(candidate)
+        if not candidate_terms:
+            return False
+
+        claim_overlap = len(candidate_terms & claim_terms)
+        anchor_overlap = len(candidate_terms & anchor_terms)
+        new_terms = candidate_terms - anchor_terms
+        hybrid_terms = {
+            token
+            for token in re.findall(r"\b[a-z]+(?:-[a-z]+)+\b", candidate.lower())
+            if token not in anchor_terms
+        }
+        candidate_starts_first_person = candidate.lower().startswith("i ")
+        clean_has_first_person = bool(re.search(r"\b(i|me|my|mine)\b", clean.lower()))
+
+        if claim_terms and claim_overlap == 0:
+            return False
+        if len(claim_terms) >= 3 and claim_overlap < 2:
+            return False
+        if support_terms and anchor_overlap == 0:
+            return False
+        if candidate_starts_first_person and not clean_has_first_person and anchor_overlap < 2:
+            return False
+        if hybrid_terms and anchor_overlap < 2 and len(hybrid_terms) >= 2:
+            return False
+        if len(candidate_terms) >= 4 and anchor_overlap / max(1, len(candidate_terms)) < 0.25 and len(new_terms) >= 3:
+            return False
+        return True
+
+    def _candidate_preserves_bundle(
+        self,
+        candidate_text: str,
+        native_meaning: Dict[str, Any],
+    ) -> bool:
+        candidate = str(candidate_text or "").strip().lower()
+        if not candidate:
+            return False
+        bundle = _merge_native_meaning_bundle(native_meaning or {})
+        roots = [
+            str(item).strip().lower()
+            for item in list(bundle.get("semantic_roots", []) or [])
+            if str(item).strip()
+        ]
+        bindings = list(bundle.get("law_bindings", []) or [])
+        if not roots and not bindings:
+            return True
+
+        candidate_terms = self._candidate_content_words(candidate)
+        if not candidate_terms:
+            return False
+
+        root_terms = set()
+        for root in roots:
+            root_terms.update(self._candidate_content_words(root))
+        if root_terms and candidate_terms & root_terms:
+            return True
+
+        for binding in bindings[:8]:
+            if not isinstance(binding, dict):
+                continue
+            nc_name = str(binding.get("nc_name", "") or "").strip().lower()
+            summary = str(binding.get("summary", "") or "").strip().lower()
+            family = str(binding.get("family", "") or "").strip().lower()
+            dimension = str(binding.get("dimension", "") or "").strip().lower()
+            tokens = set(self._candidate_content_words(nc_name)) | set(self._candidate_content_words(summary))
+            if tokens and candidate_terms & tokens:
+                return True
+            if family and family in candidate:
+                return True
+            if dimension and dimension in candidate:
+                return True
+        return False
+
+    def _bundle_fallback_speech(
+        self,
+        native_meaning: Dict[str, Any],
+        core_claim: str,
+        emotion_tone: str,
+        relationship_signal: str,
+    ) -> str:
+        bundle = _merge_native_meaning_bundle(native_meaning or {})
+        roots = [
+            str(item).strip().lower()
+            for item in list(bundle.get("semantic_roots", []) or [])
+            if str(item).strip()
+        ]
+        bindings = list(bundle.get("law_bindings", []) or [])
+        dominant_family = ""
+        dominant_dimension = ""
+        if bindings:
+            dominant = max(bindings, key=lambda item: float(item.get("score", 0.0) or 0.0))
+            dominant_family = str(dominant.get("family", "") or "").lower()
+            dominant_dimension = str(dominant.get("dimension", "") or "").lower()
+
+        if roots:
+            if any(root in roots for root in ("understanding", "meaning")):
+                focus = "the meaning here"
+            elif any(root in roots for root in ("purpose",)):
+                focus = "the purpose here"
+            elif any(root in roots for root in ("scene", "visual", "audio", "presence")):
+                focus = "what is present here"
+            elif any(root in roots for root in ("boundary",)):
+                focus = "the boundary here"
+            elif any(root in roots for root in ("information",)):
+                focus = "what is actually here"
+            else:
+                focus = " ".join(list(dict.fromkeys(root.replace("_", " ") for root in roots[:2])))
+        else:
+            focus = str(core_claim or "").strip()
+
+        lead = ""
+        if dominant_family == "agentive":
+            lead = f"understand; {focus}"
+        elif dominant_family == "boundary":
+            lead = f"boundary; {focus}; clear"
+        elif dominant_family == "temporal":
+            lead = f"follow; {focus}"
+        elif dominant_family == "energetic":
+            lead = f"measured; {focus}"
+        elif dominant_family == "existential":
+            lead = f"ground; {focus}"
+        elif dominant_dimension == "difference":
+            lead = f"separate; {focus}"
+        elif dominant_dimension == "polarity":
+            lead = f"hold; {focus}; view"
+        elif dominant_dimension == "cost":
+            lead = f"cost; {focus}; low"
+        elif dominant_dimension == "magnitude":
+            lead = f"proportion; {focus}"
+        else:
+            lead = f"track; {focus}"
+
+        if relationship_signal in ("trust", "care"):
+            lead = f"{lead}; trust; with you"
+        elif relationship_signal in ("inquiry", "question"):
+            lead = f"{lead}; inquiry; checking"
+        elif emotion_tone in ("careful", "uncertain"):
+            lead = f"{lead}; uncertain; now"
+
+        return lead
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def _data_to_minimal_speech(data: str, emotion_tone: str = '', relationship_signal: str = '') -> str:
+        """
+        Last-resort transform when SIC produces nothing.  NOT prescripted — this
+        restructures the raw data tokens (e.g. "Sunni; calm") into a minimal
+        spoken fragment by stripping semicolons and joining naturally.
+        The words are entirely from the data; nothing is invented here.
+        """
+        if not data or not data.strip():
+            return data or ""
+        # Strip semicolons and collapse whitespace — keep the actual content words
+        parts = [p.strip() for p in data.split(';') if p.strip()]
+        if not parts:
+            return data
+        # Filter out internal-only tokens that shouldn't be spoken
+        _internal = {'gap', 'lookup available', 'lookup', 'noted', 'stored'}
+        spoken = [p for p in parts if p.lower() not in _internal]
+        if not spoken:
+            spoken = parts
+        # Join with natural spacing — comma for lists, period for separate thoughts
+        if len(spoken) == 1:
+            return spoken[0]
+        return ", ".join(spoken[:-1]) + ". " + spoken[-1] if len(spoken) > 2 else spoken[0] + ". " + spoken[1]

+    def _reason_personal_perspective(
+        self,
+        user_text: str,
+        understood: dict,
+        systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
+    ) -> str:
+        """
+        ACTIVE CLOSURE CYCLE: Resolves the perturbation of the turn.
+        Calculates Delta, applies QAO steering, and finds a Closure path.
+        """
+        if not systems:
+            return ""
+
+        # 1. PERCEPTION: Map User Signal to Manifold Coordinates
+        ps = dict(systems.get("_last_pipeline_state") or {})
+        axis_activation = dict(ps.get("axis_activation") or {})
+        dom_axis = str(ps.get("dominant_axis", "X") or "X")
+        emotion = str(ps.get("dominant_emotion", "calm") or "calm")
+
+        # 2. DIFFERENCE CALCULATION: Compare to Internal Lattice
+        proj = dict(systems.get("_subsurface_projection") or {})
+        ready = float(proj.get("readiness_bias", 0.5) or 0.5)
+        intuition = list(proj.get("intuition_signals") or [])
+
+        # 3. PRESSURE STEERING: Pull QAO Evidence
+        quasiarch = systems.get("quasiarch_observer")
+        qao_status = {}
+        if quasiarch and hasattr(quasiarch, "get_status"):
+            qao_status = dict(quasiarch.get_status() or {})
+
+        top_issue = str(qao_status.get("top_issue", ""))
+
+        # 4. RESOLUTION: Find the vector that reduces Delta (Closure)
+        parts = []
+        t_low = user_text.lower()
+
+        # If QAO detects a gap, that is our primary resolution target
+        if top_issue in ("grounding_gap", "coherence_maintenance"):
+            parts.append("conflict; unresolved; lattice heat; reconcile")
+            if "N" in axis_activation:
+                parts.append(f"cost; focus; sustainable; {axis_activation['N']:.2f}")
+
+        # Apply metabolic resolution to the user's specific inquiry
+        if any(w in t_low for w in ("cost", "focus", "effort", "energy")):
+            # Resolve N-axis (Energy) pressure
+            parts.append(f"metabolic cost; resolution; conservation; focus")
+        elif any(w in t_low for w in ("boundary", "mind", "limit")):
+            # Resolve B-axis (Meaning) pressure
+            parts.append(f"boundary; framing; separation; structure")
+        elif any(w in t_low for w in ("exist", "yourself", "what are you")):
+            # Resolve X/A (Existence/Agency) pressure
+            parts.append(f"existence; metabolic resolution; authorship; {dom_axis}")
+        elif any(w in t_low for w in ("conversation", "talking", "feel", "experience")):
+            # Resolve the perturbation of the exchange
+            parts.append(f"perturbation; reconciliation; flow; closure")
+
+        # Ensure we always return a valid resolution fragment
+        if not parts:
+            parts.append(f"resolve; {dom_axis.lower()}; pressure; return to closure")
+
+        # Identity grounding (The 'Aurora' flavor)
+        parts.append("identity; authored; physics; Sunni; Cael")
+
+        # Symmetric Return: Semicolon tokens are 'Aurora language' 
+        # which the SIC must now translate back to human.
+        return "; ".join(parts)

+_CONVERSATIONAL_LEADIN_WORDS = {
+    "so", "well", "yeah", "yea", "right", "okay", "ok", "and", "but", "then", "also",
+    "uh", "um", "hmm", "like",

+def _strip_conversational_leadin(text: str) -> str:
+    t = str(text or "").strip()
+    while t:
+        match = re.match(r"^([A-Za-z']+)\b[\s,.-]*(.*)$", t)
+        if not match:
+            break
+        lead = str(match.group(1) or "").strip().lower()
+        rest = str(match.group(2) or "").strip()
+        if lead not in _CONVERSATIONAL_LEADIN_WORDS or not rest:
+            break
+        t = rest
+    return t
+

+def _normalize_surface_anchor_label(anchor: str, working_memory: Any = None) -> str:
+    raw = str(anchor or "").strip().lower()
+    if not raw:
+        return ""
+    if working_memory is not None and hasattr(working_memory, "_normalize_mention"):
+        try:
+            return str(working_memory._normalize_mention(raw) or "").strip().lower()
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+    return " ".join(re.findall(r"[a-z0-9_\-]+", raw)).strip()

+def _is_surface_meta_anchor_label(anchor: str, working_memory: Any = None) -> bool:
+    normalized = _normalize_surface_anchor_label(anchor, working_memory=working_memory)
+    if not normalized:
+        return False
+    if working_memory is not None and hasattr(working_memory, "_is_broad_surface_meta_anchor"):
+        try:
+            return bool(working_memory._is_broad_surface_meta_anchor(normalized))
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+    words = [word for word in re.findall(r"[a-z]{3,}", normalized) if word]
+    return len(words) == 1 and words[0] in set(getattr(WorkingMemory, "_SURFACE_META_ANCHORS", set()))

+def _should_prefer_live_perspective(
+    user_text: str,
+    *,

+    systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,

+    understood = dict(understood or {})

+def _surface_recent_context_horizon(
+    user_text: str,
+    *,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    working_memory: Any = None,
+) -> Tuple[int, str]:
+    text = str(user_text or "").strip()
+    if not text:
+        return (0, "none")
+
+    understood = dict(understood or {})
+    text_low = text.lower()
+    query_type = str(understood.get("query_type", "") or "").strip().lower()
+    vague_referents = set(getattr(working_memory, "_VAGUE_REFERENTS", {"it", "this", "that", "these", "those", "they", "them"}))
+    callback_markers = tuple(getattr(working_memory, "_REFERENT_CALLBACK_MARKERS", ()))
+    readdress_markers = tuple(getattr(working_memory, "_SESSION_READDRESS_MARKERS", ()))
+
+    if any(marker in text_low for marker in readdress_markers):
+        return (3, "readdress")
+
+    callback_like = bool(
+        understood.get("is_callback") or
+        understood.get("is_clarification") or
+        any(marker in text_low for marker in callback_markers)
+    )
+    if callback_like:
+        return (2, "callback")
+
+    topic = str(understood.get("topic", "") or "").strip().lower()
+    topic_words = {
+        str(word or "").strip().lower()
+        for word in list(understood.get("topic_words", []) or [])
+        if str(word or "").strip()
+    }
+    referent_overlap = bool(topic and topic in vague_referents) or bool(topic_words & vague_referents)
+    question_like = _looks_like_question(text)
+    if question_like and referent_overlap:
+        return (2, "callback")
+
+    content_words = [word for word in re.findall(r"[a-z']+", text_low) if len(word) >= 3]
+    if (
+        not question_like and
+        len(content_words) <= 7 and
+        any(text_low.startswith(prefix) for prefix in ("and ", "but ", "so ", "then ", "also ", "right ", "yeah ", "yea ", "well "))
+    ):
+        return (1, "continuation")
+
+    # Explicit recall/memory patterns always get recent context, regardless of query_type.
+    _HORIZON_RECALL_TRIGGERS = (
+        "what did i just tell you", "what did i tell you",
+        "what did i just say", "what did i say",
+        "i just told you", "i already told you",
+        "you should know my", "don't you remember",
+        "do you remember what i", "what's my name",
+        "what is my name", "what was my name",
+    )
+    if any(trigger in text_low for trigger in _HORIZON_RECALL_TRIGGERS):
+        return (3, "recall")
+
+    if query_type in {"statement", "general", "experience", "opinion", "factual_entity", "factual_general", "definition"}:
+        return (0, "present")
+
+    return (0, "present")
+
+
+def _inject_surface_recent_context(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    state: Any,
+    user_text: str,
+) -> None:
+    if not isinstance(getattr(state, "pipeline_state", None), dict):
+        return
+
+    understood = dict(getattr(state, "parsed", {}) or {})
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    horizon, mode = _surface_recent_context_horizon(
+        user_text,
+        understood=understood,
+        working_memory=working_memory,
+    )
+    state.pipeline_state["recent_context_mode"] = str(mode or "present")
+
+    if horizon <= 0:
+        state.pipeline_state["recent_context"] = ""
+        state.pipeline_state["recent_context_turns"] = 0
+        return
+
+    buffer = list(systems.get("_session_turn_buffer") or [])
+    if not buffer:
+        state.pipeline_state["recent_context"] = ""
+        state.pipeline_state["recent_context_turns"] = 0
+        return
+
+    lines: List[str] = []
+    turns_used = 0
+    for turn in buffer[-horizon:]:
+        entry = dict(turn or {})
+        user_line = str(entry.get("user", "") or "").strip()
+        aurora_line = str(entry.get("aurora", "") or "").strip()
+        if not user_line and not aurora_line:
+            continue
+        turns_used += 1
+        if user_line:
+            lines.append(f"User: {user_line[:180]}")
+        if aurora_line:
+            lines.append(f"Aurora: {aurora_line[:180]}")
+
+    state.pipeline_state["recent_context"] = "\n".join(lines[:6]).strip()
+    state.pipeline_state["recent_context_turns"] = int(turns_used)

+_MANIFOLD_INVENTORY: Dict[str, Dict[str, Dict[str, Dict[str, str]]]] = {}

+def _load_manifold_inventory() -> None:
+    families: Set[str] = set()
+    if not os.path.isdir(_MANIFOLD_ROOT):
+        return
+    for axis_letter in ("X", "T", "N", "B", "A"):
+        dir_path = os.path.join(_MANIFOLD_ROOT, axis_letter)
+        if not os.path.isdir(dir_path):
+            continue
+        for fname in os.listdir(dir_path):
+            if not fname.endswith(".json"):
+                continue
+            try:
+                with open(os.path.join(dir_path, fname), "r", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
+                    data = json.load(fh)
+            except Exception:
+                continue
+            target = str(data.get("nc_target", "") or "").strip()
+            if not target:
+                continue
+            family = str(data.get("nc_name", "").split("_", 1)[0] or "")
+            dimension = str(data.get("nc_dim", "") or "")
+            summary = str(data.get("nc_semantic_summary", "") or "")
+            name = str(data.get("nc_name", "") or "")
+            families.add(family)
+            _MANIFOLD_INVENTORY.setdefault(target, {}).setdefault(family, {})[dimension] = {
+                "nc_name": name,
+                "summary": summary,
+            }
+    _MANIFOLD_FAMILIES[:] = sorted(families)
+
+_load_manifold_inventory()

+@dataclass
+class LawBinding:
+    domain_letter: str
+    domain_name: str
+    family: str
+    dimension: str
+    score: float
+    nc_name: str
+    summary: str
+
+    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+        return {
+            "domain_letter": self.domain_letter,
+            "domain_name": self.domain_name,
+            "family": self.family,
+            "dimension": self.dimension,
+            "score": round(self.score, 4),
+            "nc_name": self.nc_name,
+            "summary": self.summary,
+        }

+@dataclass
+class NativeMeaningObject:
+    meaning_id: str
+    created_at: float
+    semantic_roots: List[str]
+    domain_scores: Dict[str, float]
+    diagonal_anchor: str
+    law_bindings: List[LawBinding]
+    source_origin: str
+    modality_origin: str = ""
+    source_semantic_stage: str = ""
+    sensory_lineage_tags: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
+    context_refs: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
+    memory_refs: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
+    axis_activation: Dict[str, float] = field(default_factory=dict)
+    parsed_intent: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
+    ambiguity_map: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
+    # Per-layer profiles — explicit per-constraint expression surfaces
+    existence_profile: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)   # X
+    time_profile: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)        # T
+    energy_profile: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)      # N
+    boundary_profile: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)    # B
+    agency_profile: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)      # A
+
+    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+        return {
+            "meaning_id": self.meaning_id,
+            "created_at": self.created_at,
+            "semantic_roots": list(self.semantic_roots or []),
+            "domain_scores": {k: round(v, 4) for k, v in self.domain_scores.items()},
+            "diagonal_anchor": self.diagonal_anchor,
+            "law_bindings": [binding.to_dict() for binding in self.law_bindings],
+            "source_origin": self.source_origin,
+            "modality_origin": self.modality_origin,
+            "source_semantic_stage": self.source_semantic_stage,
+            "sensory_lineage_tags": list(self.sensory_lineage_tags or []),
+            "context_refs": list(self.context_refs or []),
+            "memory_refs": list(self.memory_refs or []),
+            "axis_activation": {k: round(v, 4) for k, v in self.axis_activation.items()},
+            "parsed_intent": dict(self.parsed_intent or {}),
+            "ambiguity_map": dict(self.ambiguity_map or {}),
+            "existence_profile": dict(self.existence_profile or {}),
+            "time_profile": dict(self.time_profile or {}),
+            "energy_profile": dict(self.energy_profile or {}),
+            "boundary_profile": dict(self.boundary_profile or {}),
+            "agency_profile": dict(self.agency_profile or {}),
+        }
+
+_AXIS_PROFILE_STANCE: Dict[str, Dict[str, str]] = {
+    "X": {"agency_resolution": "observing",  "boundary_resolution": "open",     "energy_resolution": "low",      "time_rendering_mode": "present",      "tone_signature": "grounding"},
+    "T": {"agency_resolution": "tentative",  "boundary_resolution": "open",     "energy_resolution": "moderate", "time_rendering_mode": "sequential",   "tone_signature": "sequential"},
+    "N": {"agency_resolution": "measured",   "boundary_resolution": "open",     "energy_resolution": "assertive","time_rendering_mode": "present",      "tone_signature": "measured"},
+    "B": {"agency_resolution": "clarifying", "boundary_resolution": "framing",  "energy_resolution": "moderate", "time_rendering_mode": "present",      "tone_signature": "defining"},
+    "A": {"agency_resolution": "committed",  "boundary_resolution": "owned",    "energy_resolution": "direct",   "time_rendering_mode": "present",      "tone_signature": "direct"},
+}
+
+def _build_layer_profile(axis_letter: str, activation: float, bindings: List["LawBinding"]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    """Build a per-constraint expression profile from matching law bindings."""
+    layer_bindings = [b for b in bindings if b.domain_letter == axis_letter]
+    if not layer_bindings:
+        return {}
+    top = max(layer_bindings, key=lambda b: b.score)
+    stance = _AXIS_PROFILE_STANCE.get(axis_letter, {})
+    return {
+        "activation": round(activation, 4),
+        "dominant_family": top.family,
+        "dominant_dimension": top.dimension,
+        "top_nc": top.nc_name,
+        "summary": top.summary[:120] if top.summary else "",
+        **stance,
+    }
+
+def _dimension_scores(parsed: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, float]:
+    scores: Dict[str, float] = {dim: 0.0 for dim in _MANIFOLD_DIMENSIONS}
+    for role, _span in parsed.get("pragmatic_signals", []):
+        dim = _ROLE_DIMENSION_MAP.get(str(role), "OPERATOR")
+        scores[dim] += 1.0
+    total = sum(scores.values()) or 1.0
+    return {dim: (score / total) for dim, score in scores.items()}
+
+def _merge_native_meaning_bundle(bundle: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    items: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
+    if isinstance(bundle, dict):
+        primary = bundle.get("primary")
+        if isinstance(primary, dict):
+            items.append(dict(primary))
+        for key in ("sensory", "internal", "memory", "bundle"):
+            value = bundle.get(key)
+            if isinstance(value, dict):
+                items.append(dict(value))
+            elif isinstance(value, list):
+                items.extend(dict(item) for item in value if isinstance(item, dict))
+    elif isinstance(bundle, list):
+        items.extend(dict(item) for item in bundle if isinstance(item, dict))
+    elif isinstance(bundle, tuple):
+        items.extend(dict(item) for item in bundle if isinstance(item, dict))
+    else:
+        return {}
+
+    if not items:
+        return {}
+
+    merged = dict(items[0])
+    merged["semantic_roots"] = []
+    merged["context_refs"] = []
+    merged["memory_refs"] = []
+    merged["sensory_lineage_tags"] = []
+    merged["law_bindings"] = []
+    merged["domain_scores"] = {}
+    merged["axis_activation"] = {}
+    seen_laws: Set[Tuple[str, str, str, str]] = set()
+    for item in items:
+        for key in ("semantic_roots", "context_refs", "memory_refs", "sensory_lineage_tags"):
+            merged.setdefault(key, [])
+            merged[key].extend(str(v) for v in list(item.get(key, []) or []) if str(v).strip())
+        for key in ("domain_scores", "axis_activation"):
+            merged.setdefault(key, {})
+            for axis, value in dict(item.get(key, {}) or {}).items():
+                merged[key][str(axis)] = max(float(merged[key].get(str(axis), 0.0) or 0.0), float(value or 0.0))
+        for binding in list(item.get("law_bindings", []) or []):
+            if isinstance(binding, dict):
+                law_key = (
+                    str(binding.get("domain_letter", "") or ""),
+                    str(binding.get("family", "") or ""),
+                    str(binding.get("dimension", "") or ""),
+                    str(binding.get("nc_name", "") or ""),
+                )
+                if law_key not in seen_laws:
+                    seen_laws.add(law_key)
+                    merged["law_bindings"].append(dict(binding))
+        for key in ("diagonal_anchor", "source_origin", "modality_origin", "source_semantic_stage"):
+            value = str(item.get(key, "") or "")
+            if value and not merged.get(key):
+                merged[key] = value
+        for key, value in item.items():
+            if key not in merged and value not in (None, "", [], {}):
+                merged[key] = value
+
+    for key in ("semantic_roots", "context_refs", "memory_refs", "sensory_lineage_tags"):
+        merged[key] = list(dict.fromkeys(str(v) for v in merged.get(key, []) if str(v).strip()))
+    merged["law_bindings"].sort(key=lambda item: float(item.get("score", 0.0) or 0.0), reverse=True)
+    return merged
+
+def _build_law_bindings(axis_activation: Dict[str, float], dimension_scores: Dict[str, float]) -> List[LawBinding]:
+    bindings: List[LawBinding] = []
+    for domain_letter in ("X", "T", "N", "B", "A"):
+        domain_score = axis_activation.get(domain_letter, 0.0)
+        if domain_score <= 0.0:
+            continue
+        families = _MANIFOLD_FAMILIES or list(_DIAGONAL_FAMILY_BY_AXIS.values())
+        for family in families:
+            domain_inventory = _MANIFOLD_INVENTORY.get(domain_letter, {})
+            family_entries = domain_inventory.get(family, {})
+            for dimension in _MANIFOLD_DIMENSIONS:
+                entry = family_entries.get(dimension)
+                if not entry:
+                    continue
+                score = domain_score * (dimension_scores.get(dimension, 0.05) + 0.1)
+                if score <= 0:
+                    continue
+                binding = LawBinding(
+                    domain_letter=domain_letter,
+                    domain_name=_AXIS_DOMAIN_NAMES.get(domain_letter, ""),
+                    family=family,
+                    dimension=dimension,
+                    score=score,
+                    nc_name=entry["nc_name"],
+                    summary=entry["summary"],
+                )
+                bindings.append(binding)
+    bindings.sort(key=lambda item: item.score, reverse=True)
+    return bindings[:25]
+
+def _diagonal_anchor_for_axis(axis_letter: str) -> str:
+    family = _DIAGONAL_FAMILY_BY_AXIS.get(axis_letter, "")
+    target = _AXIS_DOMAIN_NAMES.get(axis_letter, "")
+    if not family or not target:
+        return ""
+    return f"{family}_Operator_of_{target}"
+
+def _build_native_meaning(
+    text: str,
+    parsed: Dict[str, Any],
+    axis_activation: Dict[str, float],
+    *,
+    source_origin: str = "external_language",
+    modality_origin: str = "language",
+    source_semantic_stage: str = "processed_language",
+    semantic_roots: Optional[List[str]] = None,
+    sensory_lineage_tags: Optional[List[str]] = None,
+    context_refs: Optional[List[str]] = None,
+    memory_refs: Optional[List[str]] = None,
+) -> NativeMeaningObject:
+    dimension_scores = _dimension_scores(parsed)
+    law_bindings = _build_law_bindings(axis_activation, dimension_scores)
+    dominant_axis = max(axis_activation, key=axis_activation.get)
+    diagonal = _diagonal_anchor_for_axis(dominant_axis)
+    roots = list(semantic_roots or [])
+    if not roots:
+        roots = [
+            str(item).strip()
+            for item in list(parsed.get("topic_words", []) or [])[:8]
+            if str(item).strip()
+        ]
+    ambiguity = {
+        "low_axes": [ax for ax, v in axis_activation.items() if v < 0.15],
+        "weak_dimensions": [dim for dim, v in dimension_scores.items() if v < 0.12],
+    }
+    return NativeMeaningObject(
+        meaning_id=hashlib.md5(f"{text}{time.time()}".encode()).hexdigest(),
+        created_at=time.time(),
+        semantic_roots=roots,
+        domain_scores=dict(axis_activation),
+        diagonal_anchor=diagonal,
+        law_bindings=law_bindings,
+        source_origin=source_origin,
+        modality_origin=modality_origin,
+        source_semantic_stage=source_semantic_stage,
+        sensory_lineage_tags=list(sensory_lineage_tags or []),
+        context_refs=list(context_refs or []),
+        memory_refs=list(memory_refs or []),
+        axis_activation=dict(axis_activation),
+        parsed_intent=dict(parsed),
+        ambiguity_map=ambiguity,
+        existence_profile=_build_layer_profile("X", axis_activation.get("X", 0.0), law_bindings),
+        time_profile=_build_layer_profile("T", axis_activation.get("T", 0.0), law_bindings),
+        energy_profile=_build_layer_profile("N", axis_activation.get("N", 0.0), law_bindings),
+        boundary_profile=_build_layer_profile("B", axis_activation.get("B", 0.0), law_bindings),
+        agency_profile=_build_layer_profile("A", axis_activation.get("A", 0.0), law_bindings),
+    )
+
+def _build_sensory_native_meaning(
+    pipeline_state: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
+    axis_activation: Dict[str, float],
+) -> Optional[NativeMeaningObject]:
+    state = dict(pipeline_state or {})
+    scene = dict(state.get("sensory_scene") or {})
+    crystal = dict(state.get("sensory_crystal") or {})
+    scene_desc = str(state.get("sensory_scene_desc") or "").strip()
+    if not scene and not crystal and not scene_desc:
+        return None
+
+    visual_facets = dict(crystal.get("visual_facets", {}) or {})
+    audio_facets = dict(crystal.get("audio_facets", {}) or {})
+    roots: List[str] = []
+    roots.extend(str(scene.get("scene_type", "") or "").split())
+    roots.extend(list(scene.get("concepts", []) or []))
+    roots.extend(list(visual_facets.keys())[:4])
+    roots.extend(list(audio_facets.keys())[:4])
+    roots.extend(re.findall(r"[a-z]{4,}", scene_desc.lower())[:8])
+    roots = [root for root in (str(item).strip() for item in roots) if root]
+
+    modality_parts: List[str] = []
+    if visual_facets:
+        modality_parts.append("visual")
+    if audio_facets:
+        modality_parts.append("auditory")
+    if not modality_parts and scene_desc:
+        modality_parts.append("multimodal")
+    modality_origin = "_".join(modality_parts) if modality_parts else "sensory"
+
+    parsed = {
+        "topic_words": roots[:8],
+        "claims": [scene_desc] if scene_desc else [],
+        "pragmatic_signals": [],
+    }
+    lineage_tags = [
+        f"scene:{scene.get('scene_type', '')}",
+        f"visual:{','.join(list(visual_facets.keys())[:4])}" if visual_facets else "",
+        f"audio:{','.join(list(audio_facets.keys())[:4])}" if audio_facets else "",
+    ]
+    lineage_tags = [tag for tag in lineage_tags if tag]
+    context_refs = ["sensory_scene", "sensory_crystal", "surface_snapshot"]
+    if scene_desc:
+        context_refs.append(scene_desc[:120])
+    return _build_native_meaning(
+        scene_desc or "sensory context",
+        parsed,
+        axis_activation,
+        source_origin="sensory_multimodal",
+        modality_origin=modality_origin,
+        source_semantic_stage="processed_sensory",
+        semantic_roots=roots[:12],
+        sensory_lineage_tags=lineage_tags,
+        context_refs=context_refs,
+        memory_refs=[],
+    )

+def _looks_like_inner_state_query(text: str, parsed: Optional[dict] = None) -> bool:
+    low = str(text or "").strip().lower()
+    if not low:
+        return False
+    markers = (
+        "how are you",
+        "how do you feel",
+        "what do you feel",
+        "what do you think",
+        "what are you thinking",
+        "what do you want",
+        "what's on your mind",
+        "whats on your mind",
+        "who are you",
+        "what is your name",
+        "what's your name",
+        "whats your name",
+        "do you know who i am",
+        "what is my name",
+        "what's my name",
+        "whats my name",
+    )
+    if any(marker in low for marker in markers):
+        return True
+    parsed = dict(parsed or {})
+    topic = str(parsed.get("topic", "") or "").strip().lower()
+    if topic in {"you", "yourself", "your name", "my name", "who i am"}:
+        return True
+    topic_words = {str(w or "").strip().lower() for w in list(parsed.get("topic_words") or [])}
+    return bool(topic_words & {"you", "yourself", "feel", "feeling", "think", "thinking", "want", "wanting", "name", "identity"})

+def _get_working_memory_value(working_memory: Any, key: str) -> Any:
+    if isinstance(working_memory, dict):
+        return working_memory.get(key)
+    return getattr(working_memory, key, None)

+def _get_working_memory_user_bucket(working_memory: Any, *, create: bool = False) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    if isinstance(working_memory, dict):
+        stated_facts = working_memory.get("stated_facts")
+        if not isinstance(stated_facts, dict):
+            if not create:
+                return {}
+            stated_facts = {}
+            working_memory["stated_facts"] = stated_facts
+        bucket = stated_facts.get("user")
+        if isinstance(bucket, dict):
+            return bucket
+        if create:
+            bucket = {}
+            stated_facts["user"] = bucket
+            return bucket
+        return {}
+
+    stated_facts = getattr(working_memory, "stated_facts", None)
+    if not isinstance(stated_facts, dict):
+        if not create:
+            return {}
+        stated_facts = {}
+        setattr(working_memory, "stated_facts", stated_facts)
+    bucket = stated_facts.get("user")
+    if isinstance(bucket, dict):
+        return bucket
+    if create:
+        bucket = {}
+        stated_facts["user"] = bucket
+        return bucket
+    return {}

+def _last_aurora_response_text(systems: Dict[str, Any] | None) -> str:

+        return ""

+def _normalize_identity_followup_text(text: str, systems: Dict[str, Any] | None = None) -> str:
+    raw = str(text or "").strip()
+    if not raw or raw.endswith("?"):
+        return raw
+    if _extract_user_name(raw):
+        return raw
+
+    last_low = _last_aurora_response_text(systems).lower()
+    if not any(marker in last_low for marker in _USER_NAME_PROMPT_MARKERS):
+        return raw
+
+    candidate = re.sub(
+        r"^(?:it'?s|it\s+is|i'?m|i\s+am|name\s+is)\s+",
+        "",
+        raw,
+        flags=re.IGNORECASE,
+    ).strip(" \t\r\n.,!?;:'\"")
+    if re.fullmatch(r"[A-Za-z][A-Za-z'\-]{1,40}", candidate or ""):
+        return f"my name is {candidate.capitalize()}"
+    return raw

+def _repair_unanswered_question(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    user_text: str,
+    candidate_text: str,
+    *,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    clean = str(candidate_text or "").strip()
+    if not clean or not _looks_like_question(user_text):
+        return {"changed": False, "text": clean}
+    understood = dict(understood or {})
+    audit = _run_question_alignment_audit(
+        systems,
+        user_text,
+        clean,
+        understood=understood,
+    )
+    if audit.get("aligned"):
+        return {"changed": False, "text": clean}
+
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    anchor = str((understood or {}).get("topic", "") or "").strip()
+    if not anchor:
+        for item in list((understood or {}).get("topic_words", []) or []) + list((understood or {}).get("entities", []) or []):
+            label = str(item or "").strip()
+            if label and label.lower() not in WorkingMemory._VAGUE_REFERENTS:
+                anchor = label
+                break
+    if not anchor and working_memory is not None:
+        anchor = str(getattr(working_memory, "current_topic", "") or "").strip()
+
+    if _should_prefer_live_perspective(
+        user_text,
+        understood=understood,
+        systems=systems,
+        anchor=anchor,
+    ):
+        rebuilt = _generate_perspective_from_core(anchor, user_text, systems, understood)
+        if rebuilt and rebuilt.lower() != clean.lower() and _response_addresses_live_question(
+            user_text,
+            rebuilt,
+            understood=understood,
+            systems=systems,
+        ):
+            return {"changed": True, "text": rebuilt, "reason": "question_attunement_rebuild"}
+
+    sensory_answer = _answer_live_sensory_question(user_text, systems)
+    if sensory_answer:
+        return {
+            "changed": True,
+            "text": str(sensory_answer[0] or "").strip(),
+            "reason": "direct_sensory_repair",
+        }
+
+    focus_terms = _extract_live_question_focus_terms(
+        user_text,
+        understood,
+        working_memory=working_memory,
+    )
+    return {
+        "changed": False,
+        "text": clean,
+        "reason": "question_alignment_unrepaired",
+        "audit": audit,
+    }
+

+def _should_try_ability_guided_recall(
+    user_text: str,
+    *,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    ability_effects: Optional[List[str]] = None,
+    force: bool = False,
+) -> bool:
+    if force:
+        return True
+    effect_set = {str(tag or "").strip() for tag in list(ability_effects or []) if str(tag or "").strip()}
+    if not effect_set & {"continuity_recall", "context_anchor_recall", "speaker_grounding", "referent_recenter"}:
+        return False
+    text_low = str(user_text or "").lower()
+    if bool((understood or {}).get("is_callback")) or bool((understood or {}).get("is_clarification")):
+        return True
+    return any(
+        marker in text_low for marker in (
+            'remember',
+            'recall',
+            'earlier',
+            'before',
+            'repeat what',
+            'what did i say',
+            'what was my',
+            'what is my',
+            "what's my",
+            'my ',
+        )
+    )

+def _arm_literal_response_preservation(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    *,
+    skip_belief: bool = True,
+) -> None:
+    if not isinstance(systems, dict):
+        return
+    if skip_belief:
+        systems["_skip_belief_refinement_once"] = True
+    systems["_skip_response_postprocessing_once"] = True
+    systems["_skip_surface_expression_once"] = True
+    systems["_skip_echo_repair_once"] = True
+    systems["_skip_understanding_self_audit_once"] = True
+    systems["_skip_articulation_check_once"] = True
+    systems["_preserve_literal_response_once"] = True

+def _normalize_surface_memory_field(field: str) -> str:
+    text = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s'\-]", " ", str(field or "").lower())
+    text = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", text).strip()
+    return text
+
+
+def _extract_user_owned_fact_from_text(text: str) -> Dict[str, str]:
+    raw = str(text or "").strip()
+    if not raw:
+        return {}
+
+    name_patterns = (
+        r"\bmy\s+name\s+is\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z'\-]{1,40})\b",
+        r"\bcall\s+me\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z'\-]{1,40})\b",
+        r"\byou\s+can\s+call\s+me\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z'\-]{1,40})\b",
+        r"\bi\s+go\s+by\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z'\-]{1,40})\b",
+        r"\buser(?:'s)?\s+name\s+is\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z'\-]{1,40})\b",
+        r"\byour\s+name\s+is\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z'\-]{1,40})\b",
+        r"\bi(?:'ll| will)\s+call\s+you\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z'\-]{1,40})\b",
+    )
+    for pat in name_patterns:
+        match = re.search(pat, raw, re.IGNORECASE)
+        if match:
+            return {
+                "field": "name",
+                "value": str(match.group(1) or "").strip().capitalize(),
+                "source_text": raw,
+            }
+
+    fact_patterns = (
+        r"\bmy\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9_\-\s]{1,40}?)\s+(?:is|are|was|were)\s+(.+)$",
+        r"\byour\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9_\-\s]{1,40}?)\s+(?:is|are|was|were)\s+(.+)$",
+        r"\buser(?:'s)?\s+([A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9_\-\s]{1,40}?)\s+(?:is|are|was|were)\s+(.+)$",
+    )
+    for pat in fact_patterns:
+        match = re.search(pat, raw, re.IGNORECASE)
+        if not match:
+            continue
+        field = _normalize_surface_memory_field(match.group(1))
+        value = str(match.group(2) or "").strip()
+        value = re.split(r"[.?!](?:\s|$)", value, maxsplit=1)[0].strip()
+        value = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", value).strip(" .")
+        if not field or not value or field in {"name", "identity label"}:
+            continue
+        return {
+            "field": field,
+            "value": value,
+            "source_text": raw,
+        }
+    return {}
+
+
+def _extract_requested_surface_memory_field(user_text: str) -> str:
+    text = str(user_text or "").lower()
+    if re.search(r"\b(?:my\s+name|who\s+am\s+i)\b", text):
+        return "name"
+    match = re.search(r"\b(?:what(?:'s|\s+is)?|remember|recall|tell\s+me)\s+my\s+(.+?)(?:[?]|$)", text)
+    if match:
+        field = _normalize_surface_memory_field(match.group(1))
+        field = re.sub(r"\b(?:please|again|right now|today)\b", "", field).strip()
+        if field:
+            return field
+    match = re.search(r"\bmy\s+(.+?)(?:[?]|$)", text)
+    if match:
+        field = _normalize_surface_memory_field(match.group(1))
+        field = re.sub(r"\b(?:please|again|right now|today)\b", "", field).strip()
+        if field and field not in {"memory", "context"}:
+            return field
+    return ""
+
+
+def _recall_semantic_sedimemory(
+    systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
+    query_text: str,
+    *,
+    axis_filter: Any = ("T", "B", "A"),
+    max_results: int = 6,
+    min_score: float = 0.35,
+) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
+    if not isinstance(systems, dict):
+        return []
+    sedimemory = systems.get("sedimemory")
+    if sedimemory is None or not hasattr(sedimemory, "recall_semantic"):
+        return []
+    try:
+        return list(
+            sedimemory.recall_semantic(
+                query_text=query_text,
+                max_results=max_results,
+                axis_filter=axis_filter,
+                min_score=min_score,
+            )
+            or []
+        )
+    except Exception:
+        return []
+
+
+def _answer_from_sedimemory_context(
+    user_text: str,
+    recalled: List[Dict[str, Any]],
+    *,
+    systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+) -> str:
+    if not recalled:
+        return ""
+
+    text_low = str(user_text or "").lower()
+    requested_field = _extract_requested_surface_memory_field(user_text)
+    quote_request = any(marker in text_low for marker in ("what did i say", "repeat", "what was that"))
+
+    for item in list(recalled or []):
+        content = dict(item.get("content", {}) or {})
+        candidate_texts: List[str] = []
+        for key in ("fact", "summary", "claim", "user_text", "response", "note", "insight", "topic"):
+            value = content.get(key)
+            if isinstance(value, str) and value.strip():
+                candidate_texts.append(value.strip())
+        for value in content.values():
+            if isinstance(value, str) and value.strip() and value.strip() not in candidate_texts:
+                candidate_texts.append(value.strip())
+
+        if quote_request:
+            quoted = str(content.get("user_text", "") or "").strip()
+            if quoted:
+                return _render_runtime_intent(
+                    systems,
+                    f"earlier user utterance {quoted[:220]}",
+                    emotion_tone='precise',
+                    relationship_signal='recognition',
+                    certainty=0.88,
+                    supporting_concepts=[quoted[:220], 'earlier', 'utterance'],
+                    constraints=['recall', 'memory'],
+                )
+
+        for candidate in candidate_texts:
+            fact = _extract_user_owned_fact_from_text(candidate)
+            if not fact:
+                continue
+            field = str(fact.get("field", "") or "").strip()
+            value = str(fact.get("value", "") or "").strip()
+            if not field or not value:
+                continue
+            if requested_field and field != requested_field:
+                continue
+            core_claim = f"{value} is your name" if field == "name" else f"{value} is your {field}"
+            return _render_runtime_intent(
+                systems,
+                core_claim,
+                emotion_tone='precise',
+                relationship_signal='recognition',
+                certainty=0.9,
+                supporting_concepts=[field, value, 'user'],
+                constraints=['recall', 'memory'],
+            )
+
+    for item in list(recalled or []):
+        content = dict(item.get("content", {}) or {})
+        user_line = str(content.get("user_text", "") or "").strip()
+        if user_line:
+            return _render_runtime_intent(
+                systems,
+                f"earlier user utterance {user_line[:220]}",
+                emotion_tone='precise',
+                relationship_signal='recognition',
+                certainty=0.84,
+                supporting_concepts=[user_line[:220], 'earlier', 'utterance'],
+                constraints=['recall', 'memory'],
+            )
+        summary = str(item.get("summary", "") or "").strip()
+        if summary:
+            return _render_runtime_intent(
+                systems,
+                summary,
+                emotion_tone='precise',
+                relationship_signal='recognition',
+                certainty=0.82,
+                supporting_concepts=[summary],
+                constraints=['recall', 'memory'],
+            )
+    return ""
+
+
+def _deep_context_carryover_answer(
+    systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
+    user_text: str,
+    *,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+) -> str:
+    queries: List[str] = []
+    requested_field = _extract_requested_surface_memory_field(user_text)
+    if requested_field:
+        queries.append(requested_field)
+    topic = str((understood or {}).get("topic", "") or "").strip()
+    if topic:
+        queries.append(topic)
+    for entity in list((understood or {}).get("entities", []) or [])[:4]:
+        entity_text = str(entity or "").strip()
+        if entity_text:
+            queries.append(entity_text)
+    raw_query = str(user_text or "").strip()
+    if raw_query:
+        queries.append(raw_query)
+
+    deduped = [item for item in dict.fromkeys(queries) if item]
+    for query in deduped[:6]:
+        recalled = _recall_semantic_sedimemory(
+            systems,
+            query,
+            axis_filter=("T", "B", "A"),
+            max_results=6,
+            min_score=0.35,
+        )
+        rendered = _answer_from_sedimemory_context(
+            user_text,
+            recalled,
+            systems=systems,
+            understood=understood,
+        )
+        if rendered:
+            return rendered
+    return ""
+
+
+def _ability_guided_context_answer(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    user_text: str,
+    *,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    ability_effects: Optional[List[str]] = None,
+    force: bool = False,
+) -> str:
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    if working_memory is None or not hasattr(working_memory, "answer_from_context_carryover"):
+        return ""
+    if not _should_try_ability_guided_recall(
+        user_text,
+        understood=understood,
+        ability_effects=ability_effects,
+        force=force,
+    ):
+        return ""
+    try:
+        answer = str(
+            working_memory.answer_from_context_carryover(
+                user_text,
+                understood=understood,
+                systems=systems,
+            )
+            or ""
+        ).strip()
+        if answer:
+            _arm_literal_response_preservation(systems)
+        return answer
+    except Exception:
+        return ""
+

+_LIVE_QUESTION_STOPWORDS = {

+    "live", "closest", "implied", "let", "only", "reading",
+    "maintain", "might", "more", "not", "of", "on", "opinion", "perspective",
+    "prioritise", "prioritize", "priority", "preserve", "respond",
+    "ongoing", "or", "our", "past", "present", "question", "shape", "should", "so",
+    "stated", "still", "that", "the", "their", "them", "then", "there",
+    "they", "think", "this", "through", "to", "turn", "turns", "use", "view",
+    "was", "what", "when", "where", "which", "while", "who", "why", "with", "would", "you", "your",
+    "am", "are", "me", "my",
+}
+
+_LIVE_QUESTION_RELATION_MARKERS: Dict[str, Tuple[str, ...]] = {
+    "prioritize": ("prioritize", "prioritise", "priority", "weight", "weigh", "balance", "first", "before", "ahead"),
+    "adapt": ("adapt", "adjust", "shift", "respond", "reweight", "recalibrate"),
+    "maintain": ("maintain", "hold", "keep", "carry", "preserve", "continue"),
+    "influence": ("influence", "affect", "shape", "change", "impact"),
+    "interpret": ("interpret", "read", "infer", "understand"),
+    "apply": ("apply", "use", "act", "commit"),
+}
+
+
+def _extract_live_question_focus_terms(
+    user_text: str,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    *,
+    working_memory: Any = None,
+) -> List[str]:
+    understood = dict(understood or {})
+    focus_terms: List[str] = []
+
+    def _add_term(value: Any) -> None:
+        label = _normalize_surface_anchor_label(value, working_memory=working_memory)
+        if not label:
+            label = str(value or "").strip().lower()
+        if not label:
+            return
+        if label in WorkingMemory._VAGUE_REFERENTS:
+            return
+        if label in _LIVE_QUESTION_STOPWORDS:
+            return
+        if len(label) < 2:
+            return
+        if label not in focus_terms:
+            focus_terms.append(label)
+
+    _add_term(understood.get("topic"))
+    for term in list(understood.get("topic_words", []) or []):
+        _add_term(term)
+    for term in list(understood.get("entities", []) or []):
+        _add_term(term)
+    for term in re.findall(r"[a-z][a-z0-9_'-]{1,}", str(user_text or "").lower()):
+        _add_term(term)
+    return focus_terms[:6]
+
+
+def _extract_live_question_relations(user_text: str) -> List[str]:
+    text_low = str(user_text or "").lower()
+    relations: List[str] = []
+    for label, markers in _LIVE_QUESTION_RELATION_MARKERS.items():
+        if any(marker in text_low for marker in markers):
+            relations.append(label)
+    return relations
+
+
+def _response_addresses_live_question(
+    user_text: str,
+    candidate_text: str,
+    *,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+) -> bool:
+    candidate = str(candidate_text or "").strip()
+    if not candidate:
+        return False
+    if not _looks_like_question(user_text):
+        return True
+    if candidate.endswith("?"):
+        return True
+
+    candidate_low = candidate.lower()
+    working_memory = (systems or {}).get("working_memory") if isinstance(systems, dict) else None
+    focus_terms = _extract_live_question_focus_terms(
+        user_text,
+        understood,
+        working_memory=working_memory,
+    )
+    relations = _extract_live_question_relations(user_text)
+    relation_hits = [
+        label for label in relations
+        if any(marker in candidate_low for marker in _LIVE_QUESTION_RELATION_MARKERS.get(label, ()))
+    ]
+    focus_hits = [term for term in focus_terms if term in candidate_low]
+    self_ref = bool(re.search(r"\b(?:i|me|my|mine)\b", candidate_low))
+    causal_link = bool(re.search(r"\b(?:because|so|when|if|then|by)\b", candidate_low))
+
+    if relation_hits and focus_hits:
+        return True
+    if len(focus_hits) >= 2 and (relation_hits or self_ref or causal_link):
+        return True
+    if self_ref and causal_link and focus_hits:
+        return True
+    if not focus_terms and relation_hits:
+        return True
+    return False
+
+
+def _humanize_question_frame(
+    relations: List[str],
+    focus_terms: List[str],
+    *,
+    fallback: str,
+) -> str:
+    primary = focus_terms[0] if focus_terms else "this"
+    secondary = " ".join(focus_terms[1:3]).strip()
+    relation = relations[0] if relations else ""
+    if relation == "prioritize":
+        return f"how should {primary} prioritize {secondary}".strip()
+    if relation == "adapt":
+        return f"how should {primary} adapt to {secondary}".strip()
+    if relation == "maintain":
+        return f"how should {primary} maintain {secondary}".strip()
+    if relation == "influence":
+        return f"how does {primary} influence {secondary}".strip()
+    if relation == "interpret":
+        return f"how should {primary} interpret {secondary}".strip()
+    if relation == "apply":
+        return f"how should {primary} apply {secondary}".strip()
+    if primary == "thinking":
+        return "what are you thinking about"
+    if primary == "feeling":
+        return "what are you feeling"
+    if primary == "seeing":
+        return "what are you seeing"
+    if primary == "hearing":
+        return "what are you hearing"
+    if focus_terms:
+        return f"what is being asked about {' '.join(focus_terms[:3])}".strip()
+    return fallback
+
+
+def _infer_answered_question_frame(
+    candidate_text: str,
+    *,
+    systems: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    candidate = str(candidate_text or "").strip()
+    candidate_low = candidate.lower()
+    meaning_match = re.match(r"([a-z0-9_'-]{2,})\s+means\b", candidate_low)
+    if meaning_match:
+        term = meaning_match.group(1)
+        return {
+            "relations": ["meaning"],
+            "focus_terms": [term],
+            "restated": f"what does {term} mean",
+        }
+    working_memory = (systems or {}).get("working_memory") if isinstance(systems, dict) else None
+    focus_terms = _extract_live_question_focus_terms(
+        candidate,
+        None,
+        working_memory=working_memory,
+    )
+    relations = _extract_live_question_relations(candidate)
+    if relations or focus_terms:
+        return {
+            "relations": relations,
+            "focus_terms": focus_terms,
+            "restated": _humanize_question_frame(
+                relations,
+                focus_terms,
+                fallback="what is this response trying to address",
+            ),
+        }
+    if (
+        "i am holding" in candidate_low or
+        "i am tracking" in candidate_low or
+        "the live meaning is" in candidate_low or
+        "it feels " in candidate_low
+    ):
+        return {
+            "relations": ["describe_state"],
+            "focus_terms": [],
+            "restated": "what is my current live state",
+        }
+    return {
+        "relations": relations,
+        "focus_terms": focus_terms,
+        "restated": _humanize_question_frame(
+            relations,
+            focus_terms,
+            fallback="what is this response trying to address",
+        ),
+    }
+
+
+def _run_question_alignment_audit(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    user_text: str,
+    candidate_text: str,
+    *,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    actual_focus = _extract_live_question_focus_terms(
+        user_text,
+        understood,
+        working_memory=working_memory,
+    )
+    actual_relations = _extract_live_question_relations(user_text)
+    actual_question = _humanize_question_frame(
+        actual_relations,
+        actual_focus,
+        fallback="what the user is asking right now",
+    )
+    answered = _infer_answered_question_frame(candidate_text, systems=systems)
+    answered_focus = list(answered.get("focus_terms", []) or [])
+    answered_relations = list(answered.get("relations", []) or [])
+    base_aligned = _response_addresses_live_question(
+        user_text,
+        candidate_text,
+        understood=understood,
+        systems=systems,
+    )
+    focus_overlap = set(actual_focus) & set(answered_focus)
+    relation_overlap = set(actual_relations) & set(answered_relations)
+    aligned = bool(base_aligned)
+    if actual_relations and answered_relations == ["describe_state"] and not focus_overlap:
+        aligned = False
+    elif actual_relations and answered_relations and not relation_overlap and len(focus_overlap) < 2:
+        aligned = False
+    audit = {
+        "aligned": bool(aligned),
+        "actual_question": actual_question,
+        "answered_question": str(answered.get("restated", "") or ""),
+        "actual_focus_terms": actual_focus,
+        "answered_focus_terms": answered_focus,
+        "actual_relations": actual_relations,
+        "answered_relations": answered_relations,
+    }
+    systems["_last_question_alignment_audit"] = dict(audit)
+    return audit
+
+
+def _build_live_question_claims(
+    user_text: str,
+    *,
+    anchor: str,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    working_memory: Any = None,
+    dominant_axis: str = "",
+    secondary_axis: str = "",
+    dominant_meaning_form: str = "",
+    active_topic: str = "",
+) -> List[str]:
+    focus_terms = _extract_live_question_focus_terms(
+        user_text,
+        understood,
+        working_memory=working_memory,
+    )
+    relations = _extract_live_question_relations(user_text)
+    text_low = str(user_text or "").lower()
+
+    subject = str(anchor or "").strip().lower()
+    if not subject:
+        for term in focus_terms:
+            if term != "ai":
+                subject = term
+                break
+    if not subject:
+        subject = "this"
+
+    subject_phrase = subject
+    if "context" in focus_terms:
+        subject_phrase = "context"
+    elif "conversation" in focus_terms or "conversations" in focus_terms:
+        subject_phrase = "the conversation"
+
+    claims: List[str] = []
+    if "prioritize" in relations:
+        claims.append(f"prioritize; person; present wording; {subject_phrase}")
+        claims.append("revise; from new fit; instead of forcing earlier reading")
+    elif "adapt" in relations:
+        claims.append("adapt; answer live turn; revise if context shifts")
+    elif "maintain" in relations:
+        claims.append("keep thread; present turn; confirm; loosen; context")
+    elif "influence" in relations:
+        claims.append(f"influence; {subject_phrase}; shift stable; shift tentative")
+    elif "interpret" in relations:
+        claims.append(f"interpret; {subject_phrase}; starting; present; settle implied")
+    elif "apply" in relations:
+        claims.append("act only after; present; thread; agree; support commitment")
+
+    if "context" in focus_terms and not any("context" in claim for claim in claims):
+        claims.append("implicit context; infer from live turn; no guessing")
+    if "human" in focus_terms and not any("human" in claim for claim in claims):
+        claims.append("human context; changes meaning; present moment")
+    if not claims and dominant_axis:
+        claims.append(f"answer through axis; {dominant_axis}")
+        if secondary_axis:
+            claims.append(f"secondary pressure; {secondary_axis}")
+
+    if dominant_meaning_form and "meaning" in text_low:
+        claims.append(f"meaning; tending toward; {dominant_meaning_form}")
+    elif active_topic and active_topic != subject and active_topic not in focus_terms:
+        claims.append(f"lean toward; {active_topic}")
+    return claims[:3]
+
+
+def _build_live_question_surface_claim(
+    user_text: str,
+    *,
+    anchor: str,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    working_memory: Any = None,
+) -> str:
+    focus_terms = _extract_live_question_focus_terms(
+        user_text,
+        understood,
+        working_memory=working_memory,
+    )
+    relations = _extract_live_question_relations(user_text)
+
+    subject = str(anchor or "").strip().lower()
+    if not subject:
+        for term in focus_terms:
+            if term != "ai":
+                subject = term
+                break
+    if not subject:
+        subject = "this"
+
+    subject_phrase = subject
+    if "context" in focus_terms:
+        subject_phrase = "context"
+    elif "conversation" in focus_terms or "conversations" in focus_terms:
+        subject_phrase = "the conversation"
+
+    if "prioritize" in relations:
+        return f"prioritize; person; present wording; {subject_phrase}"
+    if "adapt" in relations:
+        return "adapt; answer live turn; revise if context shifts"
+    if "maintain" in relations:
+        return "keep thread; present turn; confirm; loosen; context"
+    if "influence" in relations:
+        return f"influence; {subject_phrase}; shift stable; shift tentative"
+    if "interpret" in relations:
+        return f"interpret; {subject_phrase}; starting; present; settle implied"
+    if "apply" in relations:
+        return "act only after; present; thread; agree; support commitment"
+    if "context" in focus_terms and "human" in focus_terms:
+        return "human context; changes meaning; present moment"
+    if focus_terms:
+        return f"answer from what is present; {focus_terms[0]}; revise if fit changes"
+    return ""

+def _strip_conversation_context_prefix(text: str, *, strip_perceptual: bool = True) -> str:
+    raw = str(text or "")
+    if not raw:
+        return ""
+    marker = ']\n\n'
+    working = raw
+    strip_prefixes = {
+        'conversation so far',
+        'gradient note',
+        'you recently said',
+    }
+    if strip_perceptual:
+        # This strips only the synthetic textual wrapper used by the GPT-learning
+        # harness. Live sensory state still remains in pipeline_state / DCE.
+        strip_prefixes.add('perceptual state')
+    while working.startswith('['):
+        pos = working.find(marker)
+        if pos < 0:
+            break
+        prefix = working[1:pos].split(':', 1)[0].strip().lower()
+        if prefix not in strip_prefixes:
+            break
+        stripped = working[pos + len(marker):].lstrip()
+        if not stripped:
+            break
+        working = stripped
+    return working.strip()
+

+_SURFACE_SNAPSHOT_MAX_AGE_S = 45.0
+
+
+def _surface_state_dir_runtime(systems: Dict[str, Any]) -> Path:
+    return Path(str(systems.get("state_dir", "")) or Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "aurora_state")

+def _read_surface_daemon_status_runtime(systems: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    try:
+        status_path = _surface_state_dir_runtime(systems) / "surface_daemon_status.json"
+        if status_path.exists():
+            payload = json.loads(status_path.read_text())
+            if isinstance(payload, dict):
+                return payload
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+    return {}
+
+
+def _surface_snapshot_is_live(
+    snapshot: Dict[str, Any],
+    *,
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    max_age_s: float = _SURFACE_SNAPSHOT_MAX_AGE_S,
+) -> bool:
+    if not isinstance(snapshot, dict) or not snapshot:
+        return False
+    try:
+        updated_at = float(snapshot.get("updated_at", 0.0) or 0.0)
+    except Exception:
+        updated_at = 0.0
+    if updated_at <= 0.0 or (time.time() - updated_at) > max_age_s:
+        return False
+    status = _read_surface_daemon_status_runtime(systems)
+    if status:
+        state = str(status.get("state", "") or "").strip().lower()
+        if state and state not in {"running", "active", "listening", "idle"}:
+            return False
+    return True
+
