+def _render_live_greeting(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    *,
+    conversation_memory: Any = None,
+    working_memory: Any = None,
+    target: str = "",
+    relationship: str = "",
+    emotion_hint: str = "",
+    active_topic: str = "",
+) -> Tuple[str, str, float]:
+    snapshot = _read_surface_snapshot_runtime(systems)
+    greet_emotion = str(
+        emotion_hint or dict(systems.get("_prev_emotional_state") or {}).get("dominant", "warm") or "warm"
+    ).strip() or "warm"
+    known_name = _get_stored_user_name(conversation_memory, systems)
+    topic_now = str(
+        active_topic or (getattr(working_memory, "current_topic", "") if working_memory is not None else "") or ""
+    ).strip()
+
+    greet_concepts: List[str] = []
+    greet_parts: List[str] = []
+    target = str(target or "").strip()
+    relationship = str(relationship or "").strip()
+    sensory_recent = list(dict(snapshot.get("sensory_state", {}) or {}).get("recognitions", {}).get("recent", []) or [])
+    live_concepts = [
+        str(item).strip()
+        for item in list(snapshot.get("concepts_active") or [])
+        if str(item).strip() and str(item).strip().lower() not in {"unknown_visual", "unknown_audio"}
+    ]
+
+    if target:
+        greet_parts.append(f"{target} is here")
+        greet_concepts.append(target)
+    if relationship:
+        if target and known_name:
+            greet_parts.append(f"{target} is {relationship} to {known_name}")
+        else:
+            greet_parts.append(relationship)
+    if known_name:
+        greet_parts.append(f"{known_name} is present")
+        greet_concepts.append(known_name)
+    if greet_emotion and greet_emotion not in {"neutral"}:
+        greet_parts.append(f"feeling {greet_emotion}")
+    if topic_now:
+        greet_parts.append(f"carrying {topic_now}")
+        greet_concepts.append(topic_now)
+    if sensory_recent:
+        greet_parts.append(f"noticing {' and '.join(str(item) for item in sensory_recent[:2])}")
+        greet_concepts.extend([str(item) for item in sensory_recent[:2]])
+    elif live_concepts and (not target):
+        greet_parts.append(f"noticing {' and '.join(live_concepts[:2])}")
+        greet_concepts.extend(live_concepts[:2])
+    if not greet_parts:
+        greet_parts.append("a greeting is arriving now")
+
+    greet_claim = ", ".join(greet_parts)
+    rendered = _render_runtime_intent(
+        systems,
+        greet_claim,
+        emotion_tone=greet_emotion,
+        relationship_signal="greeting",
+        certainty=0.8 if target else 0.76,
+        supporting_concepts=greet_concepts[:4],
+    )
+    return (rendered or greet_claim, greet_emotion, 0.8 if target else 0.76)
+
+
+def _render_live_sensory_curiosity(systems: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
+    snapshot = _read_surface_snapshot_runtime(systems)
+    recent = list(dict(snapshot.get("sensory_state", {}) or {}).get("recognitions", {}).get("recent", []) or [])
+    if not recent:
+        return ""
+    lead = str(recent[0] or "").strip()
+    if not lead:
+        return ""
+    if lead.startswith("saw "):
+        claim = f"{lead}; I do not know what it is yet; what am I looking at"
+    elif lead.startswith("heard "):
+        claim = f"{lead}; I do not know what it means yet; what am I hearing"
+    else:
+        claim = f"{lead}; I do not know what to make of it yet; what should I focus on"
+    rendered = _render_runtime_intent(
+        systems,
+        claim,
+        emotion_tone="curious",
+        relationship_signal="inquiry",
+        certainty=0.7,
+        supporting_concepts=[lead],
+    )
+    rendered = str(rendered or claim).strip()
+    if rendered and not rendered.endswith("?"):
+        rendered = rendered.rstrip(". ") + "?"
+    return rendered
+

+def _read_surface_snapshot_runtime(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    *,
+    require_live: bool = True,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    try:
+        state_dir = _surface_state_dir_runtime(systems)
+        snap_path = state_dir / "surface_sensory_snapshot.json"
+        if snap_path.exists():
+            payload = json.loads(snap_path.read_text())
+            if isinstance(payload, dict):
+                if require_live and not _surface_snapshot_is_live(payload, systems=systems):
+                    return {}
+                return payload
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+    return {}

+def _answer_live_sensory_question(
+    user_text: str,
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+) -> Optional[Tuple[str, str, float, Dict[str, Any]]]:
+    raw_turn = _strip_conversation_context_prefix(user_text) or str(user_text or "")
+    text_low = raw_turn.lower()
+    snapshot = _read_surface_snapshot_runtime(systems)
+    if not snapshot:
+        try:
+            state_dir = _surface_state_dir_runtime(systems)
+            fallback_path = state_dir / "surface_sensory_snapshot.json"
+            if fallback_path.exists():
+                payload = json.loads(fallback_path.read_text())
+                if isinstance(payload, dict):
+                    snapshot = payload
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+    present = dict(snapshot.get("present_sensory_perspective") or {})
+    camera_live = bool(present.get("camera_live", snapshot.get("camera_live", False)))
+    mic_live = bool(present.get("mic_live", snapshot.get("mic_live", False)))
+    recognitions = list(dict(present.get("recognitions") or {}).get("recent") or [])
+    visual_description = str(
+        present.get("visual_description")
+        or snapshot.get("visual_description")
+        or ""
+    ).strip()
+    audio_description = str(
+        present.get("audio_description")
+        or snapshot.get("audio_description")
+        or ""
+    ).strip()
+    recent_speech = str(
+        present.get("recent_speech")
+        or snapshot.get("recent_speech")
+        or ""
+    ).strip()
+    pending_visual_question = str(
+        present.get("pending_visual_question")
+        or snapshot.get("pending_visual_question")
+        or ""
+    ).strip()
+
+    visual_query = bool(re.search(
+        r"\b(?:can|could|do)\s+you\s+see\s+me\b|"
+        r"\b(?:can|could)\s+you\s+tell\s+if\s+you\s+can\s+see\s+me\b|"
+        r"\b(?:can|could)\s+you\s+tell\s+whether\s+you\s+can\s+see\s+me\b|"
+        r"\bare\s+you\s+looking\s+at\s+me\b|"
+        r"\bwhat\s+do\s+you\s+see\b|"
+        r"\bwhat\s+are\s+you\s+seeing\b|"
+        r"\bthrough\s+your\s+(?:visual|vision|camera)\b|"
+        r"\b(?:your\s+)?visual\s+system\b",
+        text_low,
+    ))
+    audio_query = bool(re.search(
+        r"\b(?:can|could|do)\s+you\s+hear\s+me\b|"
+        r"\b(?:can|could)\s+you\s+tell\s+if\s+you\s+can\s+hear\s+me\b|"
+        r"\b(?:can|could)\s+you\s+tell\s+whether\s+you\s+can\s+hear\s+me\b|"
+        r"\bare\s+you\s+hearing\s+me\b|"
+        r"\bwhat\s+do\s+you\s+hear\b|"
+        r"\bwhat\s+are\s+you\s+hearing\b|"
+        r"\bthrough\s+your\s+(?:audio|hearing|microphone|mic)\b",
+        text_low,
+    ))
+    if not visual_query and not audio_query:
+        return None
+
+    if not snapshot:
+        if visual_query and audio_query:
+            answer = "I do not have a fresh live camera or audio read right now, so I cannot honestly tell you what I see or hear."
+            issue = 'live_multisensory_grounding_unavailable'
+            tags = ['sensory', 'vision', 'audio', 'grounding']
+        elif visual_query:
+            answer = "I do not have a fresh live camera read right now, so I cannot honestly tell you what I see."
+            issue = 'live_visual_grounding_unavailable'
+            tags = ['sensory', 'vision', 'grounding']
+        else:
+            answer = "I do not have a fresh live audio read right now, so I cannot honestly tell you what I hear."
+            issue = 'live_audio_grounding_unavailable'
+            tags = ['sensory', 'audio', 'grounding']
+        return (
+            answer,
+            "honest",
+            0.88,
+            _make_quasiarch_runtime_event(
+                target='aurora.dialogue.sensory_grounding',
+                issue=issue,
+                logic_tier='runtime_orchestration',
+                intervention='freshness_guard_answer',
+                intended_effect='prevent stale sensory claims from being presented as live',
+                observed_effect='resolved_partially',
+                tags=tags,
+            ),
+        )
+
+    if visual_query:
+        if visual_description:
+            answer = f"Through my live camera feed, {visual_description}"
+        elif camera_live and recognitions:
+            answer = f"I have a live camera feed, and right now I'm reading {recognitions[0]}."
+        elif camera_live and pending_visual_question:
+            answer = f"I have the camera feed live, but one part is still unresolved for me: {pending_visual_question}"
+        elif camera_live:
+            answer = "I have the camera feed live, but I do not have a clear visual description to give yet."
+        else:
+            answer = "My live camera feed is offline right now, so I cannot tell you what I see."
+        return (
+            answer,
+            "honest",
+            0.78 if camera_live else 0.84,
+            _make_quasiarch_runtime_event(
+                target='aurora.dialogue.sensory_grounding',
+                issue='live_visual_grounding_check',
+                logic_tier='runtime_orchestration',
+                intervention='direct_visual_grounding_answer',
+                intended_effect='answer direct visual questions from live camera state',
+                observed_effect='resolved_partially',
+                tags=['sensory', 'vision', 'grounding'],
+            ),
+        )
+
+    if audio_description:
+        answer = f"Through my live audio feed, {audio_description}"
+    elif recent_speech:
+        answer = f"I have a live audio feed. The last speech I caught was: {recent_speech}"
+    elif mic_live and recognitions:
+        answer = f"I have a live audio feed, and right now I'm reading {recognitions[0]}."
+    elif mic_live:
+        answer = "I have the microphone live, but I do not have a clear audio read to describe yet."
+    else:
+        answer = "My live audio feed is offline right now, so I cannot tell you what I hear."
+    return (
+        answer,
+        "honest",
+        0.78 if mic_live else 0.84,
+        _make_quasiarch_runtime_event(
+            target='aurora.dialogue.sensory_grounding',
+            issue='live_audio_grounding_check',
+            logic_tier='runtime_orchestration',
+            intervention='direct_audio_grounding_answer',
+            intended_effect='answer direct audio questions from live sensory state',
+            observed_effect='resolved_partially',
+            tags=['sensory', 'audio', 'grounding'],
+        ),
+    )

+# ── Aurora capability self-model map ─────────────────────────────────────────
+# Maps concept keywords → Aurora's own internal systems that embody that concept.
+# When Aurora looks up a definition, check if it describes something she already has.
+_AURORA_SELF_CAPABILITY_MAP: Dict[str, List[str]] = {
+    "context":           ["sedimemory", "working_memory", "conversation_memory",
+                          "understanding_contract"],
+    "carryover":         ["sedimemory", "understanding_contract", "working_memory"],
+    "continuity":        ["sedimemory", "understanding_contract", "conversation_memory"],
+    "memory":            ["sedimemory", "working_memory", "interaction_memory",
+                          "conversation_memory"],
+    "recall":            ["sedimemory", "working_memory", "conversation_memory"],
+    "learning":          ["chamber", "dream_trainer", "oets"],
+    "understanding":     ["understanding_contract", "oets", "working_memory"],
+    "meaning":           ["oets", "working_memory", "understanding_contract"],
+    "semantic":          ["oets", "grammar_engine"],
+    "prediction":        ["dual_strata", "prediction_field"],
+    "inference":         ["understanding_contract", "oets", "reasoning_engine"],
+    "reasoning":         ["reasoning_engine", "working_memory", "oets"],
+    "adaptation":        ["chamber", "dream_trainer", "evolution_stack"],
+    "evolution":         ["chamber", "dream_trainer", "evolution_stack"],
+    "perception":        ["perception", "sensory_integration", "sensory_crystal"],
+    "attention":         ["working_memory", "oets"],
+    "grounding":         ["oets", "sedimemory", "working_memory"],
+    "boundary":          ["foundational_contract", "constraint_stack"],
+    "agency":            ["foundational_contract", "constraint_stack"],
+    "self":              ["working_memory", "oets", "understanding_contract",
+                          "foundational_contract"],
+    "identity":          ["working_memory", "foundational_contract", "oets"],
+    "awareness":         ["working_memory", "sensory_integration", "dual_strata"],
+    "pressure":          ["lattice", "ivm", "pressure_ledger"],
+    "resonance":         ["lattice", "ivm", "dual_strata"],
+    "constraint":        ["constraint_stack", "foundational_contract"],
+}
+
+_AURORA_SYSTEM_LABELS: Dict[str, str] = {
+    "sedimemory":             "SediMemory (L3.5 stratigraphic memory)",
+    "working_memory":         "WorkingMemory (live context and facts)",
+    "conversation_memory":    "ConversationMemory (exchange history)",
+    "understanding_contract": "UnderstandingContract (intent validation loop)",
+    "oets":                   "OETS ontological web (semantic understanding)",
+    "dual_strata":            "DualStrata subsurface predictor",
+    "chamber":                "EvolutionChamber (code mutation learning)",
+    "dream_trainer":          "DreamTrainer (offline study cycles)",
+    "perception":             "PerceptionEngine (L5 expression/intake)",
+    "sensory_integration":    "SensoryIntegration (L6.5 sensory binding)",
+    "sensory_crystal":        "SensoryCrystal (audio/visual features)",
+    "reasoning_engine":       "ReasoningEngine (generative reasoning)",
+    "grammar_engine":         "GrammarEngine (discourse mode)",
+    "lattice":                "IVM lattice (5-axis pressure geometry)",
+    "ivm":                    "IVM geometry (5-axis toroidal space)",
+    "foundational_contract":  "FoundationalContract (existence boundaries)",
+    "constraint_stack":       "ConstraintStack (B/A/T/X/N gates)",
+    "evolution_stack":        "EvolutionStack (continuous improvement)",
+    "interaction_memory":     "InteractionMemory (encounter history)",
+    "pressure_ledger":        "PressureLedger (axis usage ledger)",
+    "prediction_field":       "PredictionField (DCE structured predictor)",

+def _absorb_definition_into_self_model(
+    anchor: str,
+    definition_text: str,
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+) -> Optional[str]:
+    """
+    After Aurora retrieves a Poedex definition, check if it describes a capability
+    she already possesses. If so:
+      1. Ground the concept in OETS as a semantic node with the definition.
+      2. Write a first-person self-note to working_memory mapping the concept to
+         her specific internal systems so she can refer to it in responses.
+
+    Returns a short self-referential note string if a mapping was found, else None.
+    """
+    if not anchor or not definition_text:
+        return None
+
+    anchor_low = str(anchor).lower().strip()
+    anchor_kw = set(re.findall(r'[a-z]{4,}', anchor_low))
+
+    # Find matching capability keywords
+    matched_systems: List[str] = []
+    for kw, sys_names in _AURORA_SELF_CAPABILITY_MAP.items():
+        if kw in anchor_low or anchor_low in kw:
+            for sn in sys_names:
+                if sn not in matched_systems:
+                    matched_systems.append(sn)
+        elif anchor_kw & {kw}:
+            for sn in sys_names:
+                if sn not in matched_systems:
+                    matched_systems.append(sn)
+
+    # Filter to systems that are actually present
+    present: List[str] = []
+    for sn in matched_systems:
+        if sn == "oets":
+            perception = systems.get("perception")
+            if getattr(perception, "oets", None) is not None:
+                present.append(sn)
+        elif systems.get(sn) is not None:
+            present.append(sn)
+
+    # 1. Ground in OETS
+    try:
+        perception = systems.get("perception")
+        oets = getattr(perception, "oets", None) if perception is not None else None
+        if oets is not None and hasattr(oets, "web") and hasattr(oets.web, "add_node"):
+            _node = oets.web.add_node(anchor_low, "concept", meaning=definition_text[:200])
+            if _node is not None and hasattr(_node, "add_definition"):
+                _node.add_definition(definition_text[:400], source="poedex")
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+    if not present:
+        return None
+
+    # 2. Build self-referential note
+    labels = [_AURORA_SYSTEM_LABELS.get(sn, sn) for sn in present[:3]]
+    note = (
+        f"self-knowledge; mapping; {anchor}; capabilities; "
+        f"{', '.join(labels)}; active part; how I function"
+    )
+
+    # 3. Write to working memory
+    try:
+        wm = systems.get("working_memory")
+        if wm is not None:
+            if hasattr(wm, "note_user_facts"):
+                # Use the factual note path — frame it as a first-person assertion
+                # about Aurora's own nature so it is stored as a known claim.
+                wm.note_user_facts(f"Aurora has {anchor}: {', '.join(labels)}")
+            # Also stash directly in pipeline state for next DCE evidence pass
+            _ps = getattr(wm, "_pipeline_context", None)
+            if isinstance(_ps, dict):
+                _ps["aurora_self_grounding"] = {
+                    "concept": anchor,
+                    "systems": present[:3],
+                    "note": note,
+                }
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+    # 4. Record in systems dict for this turn (DCE can pick it up from evidence)
+    try:
+        _prior = list(systems.get("_self_groundings", []) or [])
+        _prior.append({"concept": anchor, "systems": present[:3], "note": note})
+        systems["_self_groundings"] = _prior[-6:]  # keep last 6
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+    return note
+
+

+def _select_noncomp_anchor(
+    text: str,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    pipeline_state: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+) -> str:
+    understood = dict(understood or {})
+    pipeline_state = dict(pipeline_state or {})
+    vague_referents = {
+        str(item).strip().lower()
+        for item in getattr(WorkingMemory, "_VAGUE_REFERENTS", set()) or set()
+        if str(item).strip()
+    }
+    candidates: List[str] = []
+    for candidate in (
+        understood.get("topic"),
+        understood.get("search_query"),
+        pipeline_state.get("noncomp_gap_anchor"),
+        pipeline_state.get("concept_gap"),
+        pipeline_state.get("resolved_referent_topic"),
+        *(understood.get("topic_words", []) or []),
+        *(understood.get("entities", []) or []),
+    ):
+        label = str(candidate or "").strip()
+        if not label:
+            continue
+        low = label.lower()
+        if low in vague_referents or len(low) < 2:
+            continue
+        if low not in {item.lower() for item in candidates}:
+            candidates.append(label)
+    if candidates:
+        return candidates[0]
+
+    cleaned = re.findall(r"[A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9_+\-]{2,}", str(text or ""))
+    for token in cleaned:
+        if token.lower() not in vague_referents:
+            return token
+    return ""
+
+
+def _sync_noncomp_runtime_band(systems: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
+    band_pos = "inside"
+    try:
+        bias_engine = systems.get("bias_engine")
+        if bias_engine is not None:
+            band_pos = str(getattr(bias_engine, "band_position", band_pos) or band_pos)
+    except Exception:
+        band_pos = "inside"
+    nudges = dict(systems.get("_last_bias_nudges") or {})
+    router = systems.get("noncomp_manifold_router")
+    if router is not None and hasattr(router, "update_band"):
+        try:
+            router.update_band(band_pos, nudges)
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+    interpreter = systems.get("noncomp_reflexive_interpreter")
+    if interpreter is not None and hasattr(interpreter, "update_band"):
+        try:
+            interpreter.update_band(band_pos)
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+    systems["noncomp_runtime_band"] = band_pos
+    return band_pos
+

+def _stage_noncomp_prefetch(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    pipeline_state: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
+    anchor: str,
+) -> None:
+    if not isinstance(pipeline_state, dict):
+        return
+    concept = str(anchor or "").strip()
+    if not concept:
+        return
+    current_concept = str(pipeline_state.get("poedex_prefetch_concept", "") or "").strip()
+    current_status = str(pipeline_state.get("poedex_prefetch_status", "") or "").strip().lower()
+    if current_concept.lower() == concept.lower() and current_status in {"pending", "ready"}:
+        return
+
+    pipeline_state["poedex_prefetch_concept"] = concept
+    pipeline_state["poedex_prefetch_status"] = "pending"
+    pipeline_state.pop("poedex_prefetch_result", None)
+
+    def _prefetch_worker() -> None:
+        try:
+            result = ""
+            poedex_fn = systems.get("poedex") if isinstance(systems, dict) else None
+            if poedex_fn is not None and callable(poedex_fn):
+                try:
+                    result = str(
+                        poedex_fn(concept, cat="researcher", lane="self", timeout=12.0) or ""
+                    ).strip()
+                except TypeError:
+                    result = str(poedex_fn(concept, cat="researcher", lane="self") or "").strip()
+            else:
+                result = str(
+                    _try_poedex_lookup(concept, systems, timeout=2.0, use_researcher=True) or ""
+                ).strip()
+            if result:
+                pipeline_state["poedex_prefetch_result"] = result[:400]
+                pipeline_state["poedex_prefetch_status"] = "ready"
+            else:
+                pipeline_state["poedex_prefetch_status"] = "empty"
+        except Exception:
+            pipeline_state["poedex_prefetch_status"] = "error"
+
+    threading.Thread(
+        target=_prefetch_worker,
+        name=f"aurora-noncomp-prefetch:{concept[:24]}",
+        daemon=True,
+    ).start()
+
+
+def _apply_poedex_learning_result(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    concept: str,
+    request_text: str,
+    result_text: str,
+    *,
+    source_text: str = "",
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    concept_clean = str(concept or "").strip().lower()
+    request_clean = str(request_text or "").strip()
+    result_clean = str(result_text or "").strip()
+    if not result_clean or not isinstance(systems, dict):
+        return {}
+
+    learning_note = _compose_grounded_prefetch_response(concept_clean, result_clean)
+    if not learning_note:
+        first_sentence = re.split(r"(?<=[.!?])\s+", result_clean, maxsplit=1)[0].strip()
+        learning_note = first_sentence or result_clean[:240].rstrip(" ,;:")
+    if concept_clean and learning_note and concept_clean not in learning_note.lower():
+        learning_note = f"{concept_clean} learns: {learning_note}"
+
+    applied: Dict[str, Any] = {
+        "concept": concept_clean,
+        "request": request_clean,
+        "result": result_clean[:400],
+        "learning_note": learning_note[:400],
+        "applied": False,
+        "source": "poedex_learning",
+    }
+
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    if working_memory is not None:
+        try:
+            grounded = _meaning_text_is_grounded(result_clean, term=concept_clean) if concept_clean else False
+        except Exception:
+            grounded = False
+
+        if grounded and concept_clean:
+            learned = _apply_word_meaning_learning(
+                concept_clean,
+                result_clean,
+                systems,
+                source_text=source_text or request_clean,
+                source="poedex_learning",
+            )
+            if learned.get("definition"):
+                applied["applied"] = True
+                applied["definition"] = str(learned.get("definition", "") or "").strip()
+                applied["systems_updated"] = list(learned.get("systems_updated", []) or [])
+                _queue_poedex_representation_followup(
+                    systems,
+                    concept_clean,
+                    source_text=source_text or request_clean,
+                    reason="poedex_learning_result",
+                )
+                return applied
+
+        try:
+            if hasattr(working_memory, "concept_meanings"):
+                term_key = re.sub(
+                    r"\s+",
+                    " ",
+                    re.sub(
+                        r"[^a-z0-9]+",
+                        " ",
+                        f"poedex learning {concept_clean or 'material'}".lower(),
+                    ),
+                ).strip()
+                profile = _meaning_profile_for_value(learning_note)
+                concept_entry = {
+                    "term": term_key,
+                    "meaning": learning_note[:280],
+                    "contrast": "",
+                    "source": "poedex_learning",
+                    "turn": int(getattr(working_memory, "turn_count", 0) or 0),
+                    "text": request_clean[:280] or learning_note[:280],
+                    "summary": learning_note[:280],
+                    "confidence": 0.7,
+                    "verification_needed": not bool(concept_clean),
+                    "anchor_mode": "poedex_learning",
+                    "meaning_profile": dict(profile),
+                    "meaning_signature": str(profile.get("signature", "") or ""),
+                    "meaning_axes": tuple(profile.get("axes", ()) or ()),
+                    "meaning_stage": str(profile.get("stage", "") or ""),
+                    "meaning_representation": str(profile.get("representation", "") or ""),
+                }
+                working_memory.concept_meanings[term_key] = dict(concept_entry)
+                working_memory.pending_concept_clarification = dict(concept_entry)
+                working_memory.last_concept_anchor = term_key
+                if term_key not in working_memory.stated_facts:
+                    working_memory.stated_facts[term_key] = {}
+                working_memory.stated_facts[term_key]["meaning"] = learning_note[:280]
+                if hasattr(working_memory, "_register_mention"):
+                    working_memory._register_mention(term_key, "concept", "poedex_learning", 0.88)
+                if hasattr(working_memory, "_register_semantic_frame") and hasattr(working_memory, "_semantic_frame_from_concept"):
+                    try:
+                        working_memory._register_semantic_frame(
+                            working_memory._semantic_frame_from_concept(concept_entry)
+                        )
+                    except Exception:
+                        pass
+                applied["applied"] = True
+                applied["systems_updated"] = ["working_memory.concept_meanings", "working_memory.stated_facts"]
+                _queue_poedex_representation_followup(
+                    systems,
+                    concept_clean,
+                    source_text=source_text or request_clean,
+                    reason="poedex_learning_result",
+                )
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+
+    return applied
+

+def _apply_poedex_representation_result(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    concept: str,
+    request_text: str,
+    result_text: str,
+    *,
+    source_text: str = "",
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    concept_clean = str(concept or "").strip().lower()
+    request_clean = str(request_text or "").strip()
+    result_clean = str(result_text or "").strip()
+    if not result_clean or not isinstance(systems, dict):
+        return {}
+
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    if working_memory is None or not hasattr(working_memory, "concept_meanings"):
+        return {}
+
+    variants: List[str] = []
+    for chunk in re.split(r"[\n;]+", result_clean):
+        piece = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", chunk).strip(" -•\t")
+        if piece and piece not in variants:
+            variants.append(piece)
+    if not variants:
+        variants = [result_clean[:240]]
+
+    term_key = re.sub(
+        r"\s+",
+        " ",
+        re.sub(
+            r"[^a-z0-9]+",
+            " ",
+            f"poedex representation {concept_clean or 'material'}".lower(),
+        ),
+    ).strip()
+    profile = _meaning_profile_for_value(" ".join(variants[:2]) or concept_clean)
+    entry = dict(working_memory.concept_meanings.get(concept_clean, {}) or {})
+    if not entry:
+        entry = {
+            "term": concept_clean or term_key,
+            "meaning": concept_clean or term_key,
+            "contrast": "",
+            "source": "poedex_representation",
+            "turn": int(getattr(working_memory, "turn_count", 0) or 0),
+            "text": request_clean[:280],
+            "summary": request_clean[:280],
+            "confidence": 0.72,
+            "verification_needed": False,
+            "anchor_mode": "poedex_representation",
+        }
+    entry["representation_variants"] = variants[:6]
+    entry["representation_source"] = "poedex_representation"
+    entry["representation_request"] = request_clean[:280]
+    entry["representation_note"] = variants[0][:280]
+    entry["meaning_profile"] = dict(profile)
+    entry["meaning_signature"] = str(profile.get("signature", "") or entry.get("meaning_signature", "") or "")
+    entry["meaning_axes"] = tuple(profile.get("axes", ()) or entry.get("meaning_axes", ()) or ())
+    entry["meaning_stage"] = str(profile.get("stage", "") or entry.get("meaning_stage", "") or "")
+    entry["meaning_representation"] = str(profile.get("representation", "") or entry.get("meaning_representation", "") or "")
+    working_memory.concept_meanings[concept_clean or term_key] = dict(entry)
+    if hasattr(working_memory, "pending_concept_clarification"):
+        working_memory.pending_concept_clarification = dict(entry)
+    if hasattr(working_memory, "last_concept_anchor"):
+        working_memory.last_concept_anchor = concept_clean or term_key
+    if concept_clean not in working_memory.stated_facts:
+        working_memory.stated_facts[concept_clean or term_key] = {}
+    working_memory.stated_facts[concept_clean or term_key]["representation"] = variants[0][:280]
+    try:
+        if hasattr(working_memory, "_register_semantic_frame") and hasattr(working_memory, "_semantic_frame_from_concept"):
+            working_memory._register_semantic_frame(
+                working_memory._semantic_frame_from_concept(entry)
+            )
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+    try:
+        if hasattr(working_memory, "_register_mention"):
+            working_memory._register_mention(concept_clean or term_key, "concept", "poedex_representation", 0.88)
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+    systems["_poedex_representation"] = {
+        "concept": concept_clean or term_key,
+        "request": request_clean,
+        "result": result_clean[:400],
+        "variants": variants[:6],
+        "source": "poedex_representation",
+    }
+    return {
+        "concept": concept_clean or term_key,
+        "request": request_clean,
+        "result": result_clean,
+        "variants": variants[:6],
+        "systems_updated": ["working_memory.concept_meanings", "working_memory.stated_facts"],
+        "source": "poedex_representation",
+    }
+
+
+def _stage_poedex_learning_request(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    pipeline_state: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
+    anchor: str,
+    *,
+    source_text: str = "",
+    reason: str = "",
+) -> None:
+    if not isinstance(pipeline_state, dict):
+        return
+    concept = str(anchor or "").strip()
+    if not concept:
+        return
+    current_concept = str(pipeline_state.get("poedex_learning_concept", "") or "").strip()
+    current_status = str(pipeline_state.get("poedex_learning_status", "") or "").strip().lower()
+    if current_concept.lower() == concept.lower() and current_status in {"pending", "ready"}:
+        return
+
+    request_text = f"What new material should Aurora learn about {concept}?"
+    pipeline_state["poedex_learning_concept"] = concept
+    pipeline_state["poedex_learning_request"] = request_text
+    pipeline_state["poedex_learning_reason"] = str(reason or "").strip()
+    pipeline_state["poedex_learning_status"] = "pending"
+    pipeline_state.pop("poedex_learning_result", None)
+
+    def _learning_worker() -> None:
+        try:
+            result = ""
+            poedex_fn = systems.get("poedex") if isinstance(systems, dict) else None
+            if poedex_fn is not None and callable(poedex_fn):
+                try:
+                    result = str(
+                        poedex_fn(request_text, cat="researcher", lane="self", timeout=12.0) or ""
+                    ).strip()
+                except TypeError:
+                    result = str(poedex_fn(request_text, cat="researcher", lane="self") or "").strip()
+            if not result:
+                result = str(
+                    _try_poedex_lookup(concept, systems, timeout=2.0, use_researcher=True) or ""
+                ).strip()
+            if result:
+                applied = _apply_poedex_learning_result(
+                    systems,
+                    concept,
+                    request_text,
+                    result,
+                    source_text=source_text or request_text,
+                )
+                payload = {
+                    "concept": concept,
+                    "request": request_text,
+                    "result": result[:400],
+                    "note": str(applied.get("learning_note", "") or "")[:400],
+                    "status": "ready",
+                    "applied": bool(applied.get("applied", False)),
+                    "reason": str(reason or "").strip(),
+                }
+                pipeline_state["poedex_learning_result"] = payload["result"]
+                pipeline_state["poedex_learning_status"] = "ready"
+                if payload["note"]:
+                    pipeline_state["poedex_learning_note"] = payload["note"]
+                pipeline_state["poedex_learning_applied"] = bool(payload["applied"])
+                if isinstance(systems, dict):
+                    systems["_poedex_learning"] = dict(payload)
+            else:
+                pipeline_state["poedex_learning_status"] = "empty"
+                if isinstance(systems, dict):
+                    systems["_poedex_learning"] = {
+                        "concept": concept,
+                        "request": request_text,
+                        "result": "",
+                        "status": "empty",
+                        "reason": str(reason or "").strip(),
+                    }
+        except Exception:
+            pipeline_state["poedex_learning_status"] = "error"
+            if isinstance(systems, dict):
+                systems["_poedex_learning"] = {
+                    "concept": concept,
+                    "request": request_text,
+                    "result": "",
+                    "status": "error",
+                    "reason": str(reason or "").strip(),
+                }
+
+    threading.Thread(
+        target=_learning_worker,
+        name=f"aurora-poedex-learning:{concept[:24]}",
+        daemon=True,
+    ).start()
+
+
+def _stage_poedex_representation_request(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    pipeline_state: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
+    anchor: str,
+    *,
+    source_text: str = "",
+    reason: str = "",
+) -> None:
+    if not isinstance(pipeline_state, dict):
+        return
+    concept = str(anchor or "").strip()
+    if not concept:
+        return
+    current_concept = str(pipeline_state.get("poedex_representation_concept", "") or "").strip()
+    current_status = str(pipeline_state.get("poedex_representation_status", "") or "").strip().lower()
+    if current_concept.lower() == concept.lower() and current_status in {"pending", "ready"}:
+        return
+
+    request_text = (
+        f"What are other ways to represent {concept} in human language? "
+        f"Give alternate phrasing, registers, and paraphrases."
+    )
+    pipeline_state["poedex_representation_concept"] = concept
+    pipeline_state["poedex_representation_request"] = request_text
+    pipeline_state["poedex_representation_reason"] = str(reason or "").strip()
+    pipeline_state["poedex_representation_status"] = "pending"
+    pipeline_state.pop("poedex_representation_result", None)
+
+    def _representation_worker() -> None:
+        try:
+            result = ""
+            poedex_fn = systems.get("poedex") if isinstance(systems, dict) else None
+            if poedex_fn is not None and callable(poedex_fn):
+                try:
+                    result = str(
+                        poedex_fn(request_text, cat="researcher", lane="self", timeout=12.0) or ""
+                    ).strip()
+                except TypeError:
+                    result = str(poedex_fn(request_text, cat="researcher", lane="self") or "").strip()
+            if not result:
+                result = str(
+                    _try_poedex_lookup(concept, systems, timeout=2.0, use_researcher=True) or ""
+                ).strip()
+            if result:
+                applied = _apply_poedex_representation_result(
+                    systems,
+                    concept,
+                    request_text,
+                    result,
+                    source_text=source_text or request_text,
+                )
+                payload = {
+                    "concept": concept,
+                    "request": request_text,
+                    "result": result[:400],
+                    "variants": list(applied.get("variants", []) or [])[:6],
+                    "status": "ready",
+                    "source": "poedex_representation",
+                }
+                pipeline_state["poedex_representation_result"] = payload["result"]
+                pipeline_state["poedex_representation_status"] = "ready"
+                if payload["variants"]:
+                    pipeline_state["poedex_representation_variants"] = list(payload["variants"])
+                systems["_poedex_representation"] = dict(payload)
+            else:
+                pipeline_state["poedex_representation_status"] = "empty"
+                systems["_poedex_representation"] = {
+                    "concept": concept,
+                    "request": request_text,
+                    "result": "",
+                    "status": "empty",
+                    "source": "poedex_representation",
+                }
+        except Exception:
+            pipeline_state["poedex_representation_status"] = "error"
+            systems["_poedex_representation"] = {
+                "concept": concept,
+                "request": request_text,
+                "result": "",
+                "status": "error",
+                "source": "poedex_representation",
+            }
+
+    threading.Thread(
+        target=_representation_worker,
+        name=f"aurora-poedex-representation:{concept[:24]}",
+        daemon=True,
+    ).start()
+
+
+def _queue_poedex_representation_followup(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    concept: str,
+    *,
+    source_text: str = "",
+    reason: str = "",
+) -> None:
+    """
+    After Aurora learns a concept, immediately ask Poedex for alternate
+    expressions so the concept becomes usable in future interaction.
+
+    This keeps the learning loop dynamic: definition -> representation variants
+    -> stored concept meaning -> later speech.
+    """
+    if not isinstance(systems, dict):
+        return
+    concept_clean = str(concept or "").strip()
+    if not concept_clean:
+        return
+
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    if working_memory is not None:
+        try:
+            existing = dict(getattr(working_memory, "concept_meanings", {}).get(concept_clean, {}) or {})
+            if list(existing.get("representation_variants", []) or []):
+                return
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+
+    current = dict(systems.get("_poedex_representation") or {})
+    if str(current.get("concept", "") or "").strip().lower() == concept_clean.lower():
+        if current.get("status") in {"pending", "ready"} and list(current.get("variants", []) or []):
+            return
+
+    request_text = (
+        f"What are other ways to represent {concept_clean} in human language? "
+        f"Give alternate phrasing, registers, and paraphrases."
+    )
+    systems["_poedex_representation"] = {
+        "concept": concept_clean,
+        "request": request_text,
+        "result": "",
+        "status": "pending",
+        "source": "poedex_representation_followup",
+        "reason": str(reason or "").strip(),
+    }
+
+    def _worker() -> None:
+        try:
+            result = ""
+            poedex_fn = systems.get("poedex") if isinstance(systems, dict) else None
+            if poedex_fn is not None and callable(poedex_fn):
+                try:
+                    result = str(
+                        poedex_fn(request_text, cat="researcher", lane="self", timeout=12.0) or ""
+                    ).strip()
+                except TypeError:
+                    result = str(poedex_fn(request_text, cat="researcher", lane="self") or "").strip()
+            if not result:
+                result = str(
+                    _try_poedex_lookup(concept_clean, systems, timeout=2.0, use_researcher=True) or ""
+                ).strip()
+            if not result:
+                systems["_poedex_representation"] = {
+                    "concept": concept_clean,
+                    "request": request_text,
+                    "result": "",
+                    "status": "empty",
+                    "source": "poedex_representation_followup",
+                    "reason": str(reason or "").strip(),
+                }
+                return
+
+            applied = _apply_poedex_representation_result(
+                systems,
+                concept_clean,
+                request_text,
+                result,
+                source_text=source_text or request_text,
+            )
+            systems["_poedex_representation"] = {
+                "concept": concept_clean,
+                "request": request_text,
+                "result": str(result)[:400],
+                "status": "ready",
+                "variants": list((applied or {}).get("variants", []) or [])[:6],
+                "source": "poedex_representation_followup",
+                "reason": str(reason or "").strip(),
+            }
+        except Exception:
+            systems["_poedex_representation"] = {
+                "concept": concept_clean,
+                "request": request_text,
+                "result": "",
+                "status": "error",
+                "source": "poedex_representation_followup",
+                "reason": str(reason or "").strip(),
+            }
+
+    threading.Thread(
+        target=_worker,
+        name=f"aurora-poedex-representation-followup:{concept_clean[:24]}",
+        daemon=True,
+    ).start()
+
+
+def _compose_grounded_prefetch_response(anchor: str, prefetch_result: str) -> str:
+    cleaned = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", str(prefetch_result or "")).strip()
+    cleaned = cleaned.replace("**", "")
+    cleaned = re.sub(r"^[\s:;,\-]+", "", cleaned)
+    cleaned = re.sub(r"^(?:how it works|works)\s*:\s*", "", cleaned, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
+    if not cleaned:
+        return ""
+
+    first_sentence = re.split(r"(?<=[.!?])\s+", cleaned, maxsplit=1)[0].strip()
+    candidate = first_sentence or cleaned[:240].rstrip(" ,;:")
+    anchor_clean = str(anchor or "").strip()
+    if anchor_clean:
+        if candidate.lower().startswith(anchor_clean.lower()):
+            text = candidate
+        elif candidate.lower().startswith(("means ", "is ", "refers to ", "describes ")):
+            text = f"{anchor_clean} {candidate}"
+        else:
+            text = f"{anchor_clean} means {candidate}"
+    else:
+        text = candidate
+    text = re.sub(r"\s+([,.;:!?])", r"\1", text).strip()
+    if text and text[-1] not in ".!?":
+        text += "."
+    return text
+
+
+def _boot_noncomp_manifold_runtime(systems: Dict[str, Any], *, verbose: bool = False) -> None:
+    systems["noncomp_layer_compiler"] = None
+    systems["noncomp_manifold_directory"] = None
+    systems["noncomp_manifold_router"] = None
+    systems["noncomp_reflexive_interpreter"] = None
+    systems["noncomp_runtime_status"] = {"available": False}
+    systems["_last_noncomp_input"] = {}
+    systems["_last_noncomp_output"] = {}
+
+    repo_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
+    semantics_path = repo_root / "aurora_full_noncomp_rich_semantics.json"
+    manifold_dir = repo_root / "aurora_manifold_directory"
+    systems["noncomp_semantics_path"] = str(semantics_path)
+    systems["noncomp_manifold_directory_path"] = str(manifold_dir)
+
+    try:
+        if not semantics_path.exists():
+            raise FileNotFoundError(f"missing semantics file: {semantics_path.name}")
+
+        if not (manifold_dir / "_index.json").exists():
+            from aurora_constraint_manifold_compiler import compile_directory
+
+            compile_directory(
+                semantics_path=str(semantics_path),
+                output_dir=str(manifold_dir),
+                write_semantics=False,
+                only=None,
+                verbose=False,
+            )
+
+        from aurora_noncomp_layer_compiler import NonCompLayerCompiler
+        from aurora_manifold_directory_reader import ManifoldDirectory
+        from aurora_constraint_manifold_router import ManifoldRouter, build_route_index
+        from aurora_reflexive_interpreter import ReflexiveInterpreter
+
+        systems["noncomp_layer_compiler"] = NonCompLayerCompiler()
+        directory = ManifoldDirectory(str(manifold_dir))
+        router = ManifoldRouter(build_route_index(str(semantics_path)), seed=42)
+        systems["noncomp_manifold_directory"] = directory
+        systems["noncomp_manifold_router"] = router
+        band_pos = _sync_noncomp_runtime_band(systems)
+        systems["noncomp_reflexive_interpreter"] = ReflexiveInterpreter(
+            directory=directory,
+            router=router,
+            band_pos=band_pos,
+        )
+        systems["noncomp_runtime_status"] = {
+            "available": True,
+            "band_pos": band_pos,
+            "directory_entries": int(getattr(directory, "total", 0) or 0),
+            "semantics_path": str(semantics_path),
+            "manifold_dir": str(manifold_dir),
+        }
+        if verbose:
+            print(
+                "  [NONCOMP] Manifold runtime active "
+                f"({systems['noncomp_runtime_status']['directory_entries']} noncomp manifolds)"
+            )
+    except Exception as noncomp_exc:
+        systems["noncomp_runtime_status"] = {
+            "available": False,
+            "reason": str(noncomp_exc),
+            "semantics_path": str(semantics_path),
+            "manifold_dir": str(manifold_dir),
+        }
+        if verbose:
+            print(f"  [NONCOMP] Manifold runtime unavailable: {noncomp_exc}")
+
+
+def _apply_noncomp_input_guidance(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    state: Any,
+    user_text: str,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    interpreter = systems.get("noncomp_reflexive_interpreter")
+    if interpreter is None or not hasattr(interpreter, "interpret"):
+        return {}
+
+    band_pos = _sync_noncomp_runtime_band(systems)
+    pipeline_state = getattr(state, "pipeline_state", None)
+    understood = dict(getattr(state, "parsed", {}) or {})
+    anchor = _select_noncomp_anchor(user_text, understood=understood, pipeline_state=pipeline_state)
+    try:
+        summary = dict(interpreter.interpret(user_text).to_dict() or {})
+    except Exception:
+        return {}
+
+    summary["context"] = "input"
+    summary["band_pos"] = band_pos
+    summary["anchor"] = anchor
+    prefer_live_perspective = _should_prefer_live_perspective(
+        user_text,
+        understood=understood,
+        systems=systems,
+        anchor=anchor,
+    )
+
+    callback_like = bool(understood.get("is_callback") or understood.get("is_clarification"))
+    lower_text = str(user_text or "").lower()
+    definition_like = bool(_extract_inline_lookup_targets(user_text)) or any(
+        phrase in lower_text for phrase in (
+            "what does ",
+            "what do you mean by ",
+            "what does that mean",
+            "what does this mean",
+            "tell me what ",
+            "look up what ",
+        )
+    )
+    needs_remedy = (
+        not bool(summary.get("is_understood")) or
+        str(summary.get("field_region", "") or "") == "sparse" or
+        not bool(summary.get("polarity_coherent", True))
+    )
+    if prefer_live_perspective:
+        needs_remedy = False
+    if definition_like and anchor:
+        needs_remedy = True
+    if needs_remedy:
+        if definition_like and anchor:
+            remedy = "lookup"
+        elif callback_like or not anchor:
+            remedy = "clarify"
+        elif _looks_like_question(user_text):
+            remedy = "lookup"
+        else:
+            remedy = "clarify"
+    else:
+        remedy = "none"
+    summary["needs_remedy"] = needs_remedy
+    summary["remedy"] = remedy
+    summary["prefer_live_perspective"] = bool(prefer_live_perspective)
+
+    state.noncomp_input_state = dict(summary)
+    if isinstance(pipeline_state, dict):
+        pipeline_state["noncomp_input"] = dict(summary)
+        if anchor:
+            pipeline_state["noncomp_anchor"] = anchor
+        if needs_remedy:
+            pipeline_state["noncomp_should_seek_remedy"] = True
+            pipeline_state["noncomp_remedy"] = remedy
+            if anchor:
+                pipeline_state.setdefault("concept_gap", anchor)
+                pipeline_state["noncomp_gap_anchor"] = anchor
+    systems["_last_noncomp_input"] = dict(summary)
+
+    if needs_remedy and remedy == "lookup" and anchor:
+        _stage_noncomp_prefetch(systems, pipeline_state, anchor)
+        _stage_poedex_learning_request(
+            systems,
+            pipeline_state,
+            anchor,
+            source_text=user_text,
+            reason="noncomp_lookup_gap",
+        )
+
+    return summary
+
+
+def _apply_noncomp_output_guidance(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    state: Any,
+    user_text: str,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    interpreter = systems.get("noncomp_reflexive_interpreter")
+    response_text = str(getattr(state, "response_content", "") or "").strip()
+    if interpreter is None or not hasattr(interpreter, "interpret") or not response_text:
+        return {}
+
+    band_pos = _sync_noncomp_runtime_band(systems)
+    pipeline_state = getattr(state, "pipeline_state", None)
+    input_summary = dict(getattr(state, "noncomp_input_state", {}) or systems.get("_last_noncomp_input") or {})
+    actuation = dict(input_summary.get("behavior_actuation", {}) or {})
+    actuation_flags = {str(flag or "").strip() for flag in list(actuation.get("flags", []) or []) if str(flag or "").strip()}
+    anchor = str(
+        input_summary.get("anchor", "") or
+        _select_noncomp_anchor(user_text, understood=getattr(state, "parsed", {}), pipeline_state=pipeline_state)
+    ).strip()
+
+    try:
+        summary = dict(interpreter.interpret(response_text).to_dict() or {})
+    except Exception:
+        return {}
+
+    summary["context"] = "output"
+    summary["band_pos"] = band_pos
+    summary["anchor"] = anchor
+    needs_grounding = (
+        not bool(summary.get("is_understood")) or
+        str(summary.get("field_region", "") or "") == "sparse" or
+        not bool(summary.get("polarity_coherent", True))
+    )
+    if "prefer_lookup_grounding" in actuation_flags and len(response_text.split()) <= 12:
+        needs_grounding = True
+    summary["needs_grounding"] = needs_grounding
+
+    state.noncomp_output_state = dict(summary)
+    if isinstance(pipeline_state, dict):
+        pipeline_state["noncomp_output"] = dict(summary)
+        if needs_grounding:
+            pipeline_state["noncomp_output_needs_grounding"] = True
+    systems["_last_noncomp_output"] = dict(summary)
+
+    if "prefer_low_assertion" in actuation_flags:
+        state.response_confidence = min(
+            float(getattr(state, "response_confidence", 0.5) or 0.5),
+            0.72,
+        )
+        if str(getattr(state, "response_tone", "neutral") or "neutral") in {"neutral", "informative", "direct", "assertive"}:
+            state.response_tone = "careful"
+
+    if "prefer_concise_response" in actuation_flags and len(response_text.split()) > 60:
+        sentences = re.split(r"(?<=[.!?])\s+", response_text)
+        shortened = " ".join(sentences[:2]).strip()
+        if shortened and len(shortened.split()) >= 8:
+            state.response_content = shortened
+            response_text = shortened
+
+    if not needs_grounding:
+        return summary
+
+    state.response_confidence = min(
+        float(getattr(state, "response_confidence", 0.5) or 0.5),
+        0.68 if not bool(summary.get("is_understood")) else 0.74,
+    )
+    if str(getattr(state, "response_tone", "neutral") or "neutral") in {
+        "neutral", "informative", "direct", "assertive"
+    }:
+        state.response_tone = "careful" if not bool(summary.get("is_understood")) else "reflective"
+
+    prefetch_result = ""
+    if isinstance(pipeline_state, dict):
+        prefetch_result = str(pipeline_state.get("poedex_prefetch_result", "") or "").strip()
+
+    changed = False
+    if prefetch_result and len(response_text.split()) <= 8:
+        grounded_prefetch = _compose_grounded_prefetch_response(anchor, prefetch_result[:480])
+        if grounded_prefetch and len(grounded_prefetch.split()) >= 4:
+            state.response_content = grounded_prefetch
+            changed = True
+        else:
+            rerendered = _render_runtime_intent(
+                systems,
+                prefetch_result[:480],
+                emotion_tone=str(getattr(state, "response_tone", "careful") or "careful"),
+                certainty=float(getattr(state, "response_confidence", 0.62) or 0.62),
+                supporting_concepts=[anchor] if anchor else [],
+            )
+            if rerendered and len(rerendered.split()) >= 4:
+                state.response_content = rerendered
+                changed = True
+    elif anchor and len(response_text.split()) <= 3:
+        rerendered = _render_runtime_intent(
+            systems,
+            f"{anchor}; {response_text}",
+            emotion_tone=str(getattr(state, "response_tone", "careful") or "careful"),
+            certainty=float(getattr(state, "response_confidence", 0.58) or 0.58),
+            supporting_concepts=[anchor],
+        )
+        if rerendered and len(rerendered.split()) >= max(4, len(response_text.split()) + 1):
+            state.response_content = rerendered
+            changed = True
+
+    if changed:
+        summary["regrounded"] = True
+        state.noncomp_output_state = dict(summary)
+        if isinstance(pipeline_state, dict):
+            pipeline_state["noncomp_output"] = dict(summary)
+            pipeline_state["noncomp_output_regrounded"] = True
+        systems["_last_noncomp_output"] = dict(summary)
+        try:
+            repaired, tone2, conf2, _ = _repair_discourse_coherence(
+                str(getattr(state, "response_content", "") or ""),
+                str(getattr(state, "response_tone", "careful") or "careful"),
+                float(getattr(state, "response_confidence", 0.58) or 0.58),
+                user_text,
+                systems,
+                understood=dict(getattr(state, "parsed", {}) or {}),
+            )
+            state.response_content = repaired
+            state.response_tone = tone2
+            state.response_confidence = conf2
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+
+    return summary
+
+
+def _extract_inline_lookup_targets(text: str) -> List[str]:
+    low = str(text or "").strip().lower()
+    if not low:
+        return []
+    targets: List[str] = []
+    patterns = (
+        r"\bwhat\s+does\s+([a-z0-9][a-z0-9_+\-]{0,31})\s+mean\b",
+        r"\bwhat\s+do\s+you\s+mean\s+by\s+([a-z0-9][a-z0-9_+\-\s]{0,40})\b",
+        r"\blook\s+up\s+what\s+([a-z0-9][a-z0-9_+\-]{0,31})\s+means\b",
+        r"\btell\s+me\s+what\s+([a-z0-9][a-z0-9_+\-]{0,31})\s+means\b",
+        r"\byou\s+know\s+what\s+([a-z0-9][a-z0-9_+\-]{0,31})\s+means\b",
+        r"\bdo\s+you\s+know\s+what\s+([a-z0-9][a-z0-9_+\-]{0,31})\s+means\b",
+        r"\b([a-z0-9][a-z0-9_+\-]{0,31})\s+means\s+what\b",
+        r"\bdefine\s+([a-z0-9][a-z0-9_+\-\s]{0,40})\b",
+        r"\bdefinition\s+of\s+([a-z0-9][a-z0-9_+\-\s]{0,40})\b",
+    )
+    for pattern in patterns:
+        for match in re.finditer(pattern, low, re.IGNORECASE):
+            token = str(match.group(1) or "").strip(" .,!?:;\"'()[]{}").lower()
+            if token and token not in targets:
+                targets.append(token)
+    return targets[:3]
+
+
+def _meaning_text_is_grounded(definition: str, *, term: str = "") -> bool:
+    clean = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", str(definition or "")).strip(" \t\r\n.,;:!?")
+    if not clean:
+        return False
+    low = clean.lower()
+    term_low = str(term or "").strip().lower()
+    if low.startswith("learned:"):
+        return False
+    if low in {"unknown", "n/a", "tbd", "pending", "is:**", "works:**"}:
+        return False
+    if term_low and low in {term_low, f'"{term_low}"', f"'{term_low}'"}:
+        return False
+    return True
+
+
+def _lookup_local_grounded_definition(term: str, systems: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
+    clean_term = str(term or "").strip()
+    if not clean_term or not isinstance(systems, dict):
+        return ""
+
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    concept_meanings = getattr(working_memory, "concept_meanings", {}) if working_memory is not None else {}
+    for key in (clean_term, clean_term.lower(), clean_term.capitalize()):
+        concept = dict(concept_meanings.get(key, {}) or {})
+        meaning = str(concept.get("meaning", "") or "").strip()
+        if _meaning_text_is_grounded(meaning, term=clean_term):
+            return meaning
+
+    perception = systems.get("perception")
+    lexicon = getattr(perception, "lexicon", None) if perception is not None else None
+    entries = getattr(lexicon, "entries", {}) if lexicon is not None else {}
+    for key in (clean_term, clean_term.lower(), clean_term.capitalize()):
+        entry = entries.get(key)
+        if entry is None:
+            continue
+        if isinstance(entry, dict):
+            meaning = str(entry.get("meaning", "") or "").strip()
+        else:
+            meaning = str(getattr(entry, "meaning", "") or "").strip()
+        if _meaning_text_is_grounded(meaning, term=clean_term):
+            return meaning
+
+    oets = getattr(perception, "oets", None) if perception is not None else None
+    web = getattr(oets, "web", None) if oets is not None else None
+    if web is None:
+        return ""
+
+    node = None
+    for key in (clean_term, clean_term.lower(), clean_term.capitalize()):
+        try:
+            if hasattr(web, "has_node") and web.has_node(key):
+                node = web.get_node(key)
+                break
+        except Exception:
+            continue
+    if node is None:
+        return ""
+
+    candidates: List[str] = []
+    direct_meaning = str(getattr(node, "meaning", "") or "").strip()
+    if direct_meaning:
+        candidates.append(direct_meaning)
+    for item in list(getattr(node, "definitions", []) or []):
+        if isinstance(item, dict):
+            for key in ("definition", "text", "meaning", "content"):
+                value = str(item.get(key, "") or "").strip()
+                if value:
+                    candidates.append(value)
+        else:
+            for attr in ("definition", "text", "meaning", "content"):
+                value = str(getattr(item, attr, "") or "").strip()
+                if value:
+                    candidates.append(value)
+            value = str(item or "").strip()
+            if value:
+                candidates.append(value)
+    for candidate in candidates:
+        if _meaning_text_is_grounded(candidate, term=clean_term):
+            return candidate
+    return ""
+
+
+def _definition_lookup_target(
+    user_text: str,
+    *,
+    understood: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
+    fallback: str = "",
+) -> str:
+    explicit_targets = _extract_inline_lookup_targets(user_text)
+    if explicit_targets:
+        return str(explicit_targets[0] or "").strip().lower()
+
+    low = str(user_text or "").strip().lower()
+    query_type = str(((understood or {}).get("query_type", "") if isinstance(understood, dict) else "") or "").strip().lower()
+    candidate = str(fallback or "").strip(" \t\r\n.,;:!?\"'()[]{}").lower()
+    if not candidate:
+        return ""
+
+    weak_labels = set(_GROUNDING_FALLBACK_SKIP) | {
+        "that", "this", "it", "thing", "stuff", "someone", "somebody",
+        "mean", "means", "meaning", "define", "definition",
+    }
+    if candidate in weak_labels:
+        return ""
+
+    if (
+        "mean by" in low or
+        low.startswith("define ") or
+        " definition of " in f" {low} " or
+        ("mean" in low and query_type in {"definition", "clarification"})
+    ):
+        return candidate
+    return ""
+
+
+def _apply_word_meaning_learning(
+    term: str,
+    lookup_text: str,
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    *,
+    source_text: str = "",
+    source: str = "poedex",
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    clean_term = str(term or "").strip().lower()
+    raw_lookup = str(lookup_text or "").strip()
+    if not clean_term or not raw_lookup or not isinstance(systems, dict):
+        return {}
+
+    try:
+        from aurora_internal.aurora_comprehension_gap import (
+            ComprehensionGap,
+            GapResolutionApplicator,
+            GapType,
+        )
+    except Exception:
+        return {}
+
+    applicator = GapResolutionApplicator()
+    extracted = str(applicator._extract_definition(clean_term, raw_lookup) or "").strip()
+    definition = extracted if _meaning_text_is_grounded(extracted, term=clean_term) else raw_lookup
+    if not _meaning_text_is_grounded(definition, term=clean_term):
+        return {}
+
+    gap = ComprehensionGap(
+        gap_id=f"inline_vocab_{clean_term}_{time.time():.6f}",
+        gap_type=GapType.VOCABULARY,
+        unclear_element=clean_term,
+        source_text=str(source_text or clean_term),
+        question="",
+        confidence_before=0.2,
+        pending=False,
+        resolution_text=raw_lookup,
+    )
+    resolved = applicator.apply(gap, systems)
+
+    gap_system = systems.get("_comprehension_gap") or systems.get("comprehension_gap_system")
+    gap_memory = getattr(gap_system, "memory", None)
+    if gap_memory is not None and hasattr(gap_memory, "store_resolved"):
+        try:
+            gap_memory.store_resolved(resolved)
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    concept = None
+    if working_memory is not None:
+        next_turn = int(getattr(working_memory, "turn_count", 0) or 0) + 1
+        understood = {
+            "topic": clean_term,
+            "topic_words": [clean_term],
+            "entities": [clean_term],
+            "query_type": "clarification",
+            "is_clarification": True,
+        }
+        if hasattr(working_memory, "note_concept_clarification"):
+            try:
+                working_memory.note_concept_clarification(
+                    f"{clean_term} means {definition}",
+                    source=source,
+                    understood=understood,
+                )
+            except Exception:
+                pass
+        try:
+            if clean_term in getattr(working_memory, "concept_meanings", {}):
+                working_memory.concept_meanings[clean_term]["turn"] = next_turn
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+        try:
+            concept_meanings = getattr(working_memory, "concept_meanings", None)
+            if isinstance(concept_meanings, dict) and clean_term not in concept_meanings:
+                profile = _meaning_profile_for_value(definition)
+                concept = {
+                    "term": clean_term,
+                    "meaning": definition,
+                    "contrast": "",
+                    "source": source,
+                    "turn": next_turn,
+                    "text": str(source_text or f"{clean_term} means {definition}")[:280],
+                    "summary": f"{clean_term} means {definition}",
+                    "confidence": 0.9,
+                    "verification_needed": False,
+                    "anchor_mode": "poedex_lookup" if source == "poedex" else "grounded_definition",
+                    "meaning_profile": dict(profile),
+                    "meaning_signature": str(profile.get("signature", "") or ""),
+                    "meaning_axes": tuple(profile.get("axes", ()) or ()),
+                    "meaning_stage": str(profile.get("stage", "") or ""),
+                    "meaning_representation": str(profile.get("representation", "") or ""),
+                }
+                concept_meanings[clean_term] = dict(concept)
+                if hasattr(working_memory, "pending_concept_clarification"):
+                    working_memory.pending_concept_clarification = dict(concept)
+                if hasattr(working_memory, "last_concept_anchor"):
+                    working_memory.last_concept_anchor = clean_term
+                try:
+                    stated_facts = getattr(working_memory, "stated_facts", None)
+                    if isinstance(stated_facts, dict):
+                        if clean_term not in stated_facts:
+                            stated_facts[clean_term] = {}
+                        stated_facts[clean_term]["meaning"] = definition
+                except Exception:
+                    pass
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+        try:
+            if hasattr(working_memory, "_register_mention"):
+                working_memory._register_mention(clean_term, "concept", source, 0.94)
+                for idx, word in enumerate(re.findall(r"[a-z]{3,}", definition.lower())[:4]):
+                    if not getattr(working_memory, "_is_weak_anchor_label", lambda _w: False)(word):
+                        working_memory._register_mention(
+                            word,
+                            "meaning",
+                            source,
+                            max(0.44, 0.78 - idx * 0.08),
+                        )
+            if (
+                concept is not None
+                and hasattr(working_memory, "_semantic_frame_from_concept")
+                and hasattr(working_memory, "_register_semantic_frame")
+            ):
+                working_memory._register_semantic_frame(
+                    working_memory._semantic_frame_from_concept(concept)
+                )
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+    _queue_poedex_representation_followup(
+        systems,
+        clean_term,
+        source_text=source_text or f"{clean_term} means {definition}",
+        reason=f"{source}_definition_learning",
+    )
+
+    systems["_inline_vocab_lookup"] = {
+        "source_text": str(source_text or clean_term),
+        "count": 1,
+        "applied": [{
+            "word": clean_term,
+            "definition": definition[:240],
+            "systems_updated": list(getattr(resolved, "systems_updated", []) or []),
+            "source": source,
+        }],
+        "grounded_text": f"{str(source_text or clean_term).strip()}. {clean_term} means {definition}.",
+    }
+    return {
+        "word": clean_term,
+        "definition": definition,
+        "systems_updated": list(getattr(resolved, "systems_updated", []) or []),
+        "source": source,
+    }
+
+
+def _render_learned_definition_response(
+    term: str,
+    definition: str,
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    *,
+    certainty: float = 0.82,
+    emotion_tone: str = "attentive",
+) -> str:
+    clean_term = str(term or "").strip().lower()
+    clean_definition = str(definition or "").strip()
+    grounded_definition = _compose_grounded_prefetch_response(clean_term, clean_definition)
+    rendered_definition = _render_runtime_intent(
+        systems,
+        (grounded_definition or f"{clean_term} means {clean_definition}").rstrip("."),
+        emotion_tone=emotion_tone,
+        certainty=certainty,
+        supporting_concepts=[clean_term, clean_definition],
+        constraints=["meaning", "vocabulary"],
+    )
+    return str(
+        rendered_definition or grounded_definition or f"{clean_term} means {clean_definition}."
+    ).strip()
+
+
+def _repair_unknown_vocabulary_inline(
+    user_text: str,
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    *,
+    max_terms: int = 2,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    text = str(user_text or "").strip()
+    if not text or not isinstance(systems, dict):
+        return {}
+    try:
+        from aurora_internal.aurora_comprehension_gap import (
+            ComprehensionGap,
+            GapResolutionApplicator,
+            GapType,
+            VolatilityDetector,
+        )
+    except Exception:
+        return {}
+
+    perception = systems.get("perception")
+    lexicon = getattr(perception, "lexicon", None) if perception else None
+    oets = getattr(perception, "oets", None) if perception else None
+    report = VolatilityDetector().detect(text, lexicon=lexicon, oets=oets)
+    unknown_words = list(report.get("unknown_words") or [])
+    for explicit_target in _extract_inline_lookup_targets(text):
+        if explicit_target not in unknown_words:
+            unknown_words.append(explicit_target)
+    if not unknown_words:
+        return {}
+
+    stated_name = _extract_user_name(text)
+    skipped = {stated_name.lower()} if stated_name else set()
+    gap_system = systems.get("_comprehension_gap") or systems.get("comprehension_gap_system")
+    gap_memory = getattr(gap_system, "memory", None)
+    applicator = GapResolutionApplicator()
+    applied: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
+
+    for word in unknown_words:
+        token = str(word or "").strip().lower()
+        if not token or token in skipped:
+            continue
+        source = "local_definition"
+        lookup = str(_lookup_local_grounded_definition(token, systems) or "").strip()
+        if not lookup:
+            source = "poedex"
+            lookup = str(
+                _try_poedex_lookup(token, systems, timeout=2.0, use_researcher=True) or ""
+            ).strip()
+        if not _meaning_text_is_grounded(lookup, term=token):
+            continue
+        learned = _apply_word_meaning_learning(
+            token,
+            lookup,
+            systems,
+            source_text=text,
+            source=source,
+        )
+        definition = str(learned.get("definition", "") or "").strip()
+        if not _meaning_text_is_grounded(definition, term=token):
+            definition = str(applicator._extract_definition(token, lookup) or lookup).strip()
+        if not _meaning_text_is_grounded(definition, term=token):
+            continue
+        applied.append({
+            "word": token,
+            "definition": definition[:240],
+            "systems_updated": list(learned.get("systems_updated", []) or []),
+            "source": source,
+        })
+        if len(applied) >= max_terms:
+            break
+
+    if not applied:
+        return {}
+    grounded_text = text
+    glosses = []
+    for item in applied:
+        word = str(item.get("word", "") or "").strip()
+        definition = str(item.get("definition", "") or "").strip()
+        if word and definition:
+            glosses.append(f"{word} means {definition}")
+    if glosses:
+        grounded_text = f"{text}. " + ". ".join(glosses) + "."
+    systems["_inline_vocab_lookup"] = {
+        "source_text": text,
+        "count": len(applied),
+        "applied": applied,
+        "grounded_text": grounded_text,
+    }
+    return dict(systems["_inline_vocab_lookup"])
+

+def _resolve_passive_ability_effect_owner(tag: str) -> str:
+    clean = str(tag or "").strip()
+    if not clean:
+        return ""
+    owner = str(_ABILITY_EFFECT_PASSIVE_OWNERS.get(clean, "") or "").strip()
+    if owner:
+        return owner
+    owner = str(_ABILITY_EFFECT_PRIMITIVE_OWNERS.get(clean, "") or "").strip()
+    if owner:
+        return owner
+    for prefix, passive_owner in _ABILITY_EFFECT_PASSIVE_PREFIX_OWNERS.items():
+        if clean.startswith(prefix):
+            return passive_owner
+    return ""
