+def _summarize_live_ability_effects(effect_tags: List[str]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    raw_effects: List[str] = []
+    seen_raw = set()
+    for tag in list(effect_tags or []):
+        clean = str(tag or "").strip()
+        if not clean or clean in seen_raw:
+            continue
+        seen_raw.add(clean)
+        raw_effects.append(clean)
+
+    expanded_effects: List[str] = []
+    seen_expanded = set()
+    translated_effects: Dict[str, List[str]] = {}
+
+    def _push(label: str) -> None:
+        clean = str(label or "").strip()
+        if not clean or clean in seen_expanded:
+            return
+        seen_expanded.add(clean)
+        expanded_effects.append(clean)
+
+    for tag in raw_effects:
+        _push(tag)
+        aliases = [
+            str(alias or "").strip()
+            for alias in _ABILITY_EFFECT_ALIAS_MAP.get(tag, ())
+            if str(alias or "").strip()
+        ]
+        if aliases:
+            translated_effects[tag] = aliases
+        for alias in aliases:
+            _push(alias)
+
+    translated_roots = set(translated_effects)
+    handled_effects: List[str] = []
+    passive_effects: List[Dict[str, str]] = []
+    unhandled_effects: List[str] = []
+    for tag in expanded_effects:
+        if tag in translated_roots:
+            continue
+        if tag in _ABILITY_EFFECT_RUNTIME_HANDLERS:
+            handled_effects.append(tag)
+            continue
+        owner = _resolve_passive_ability_effect_owner(tag)
+        if owner:
+            passive_effects.append({"tag": tag, "owner": owner})
+            continue
+        unhandled_effects.append(tag)
+
+    effect_set = set(expanded_effects)
+    runtime_flags = {
+        "force_continuity_recall": bool(effect_set & {"continuity_recall", "context_anchor_recall"}),
+        "prefer_speaker_grounding": bool(effect_set & {"speaker_grounding", "referent_recenter"}),
+        "prefer_conflict_surface": bool(effect_set & {"resolve", "merge_conflict"}),
+        "has_unhandled_effects": bool(unhandled_effects),
+    }
+    return {
+        "raw_effects": raw_effects,
+        "expanded_effects": expanded_effects,
+        "translated_effects": translated_effects,
+        "handled_effects": handled_effects,
+        "passive_effects": passive_effects,
+        "unhandled_effects": unhandled_effects,
+        "runtime_flags": runtime_flags,
+    }
+
+
+_NONCOMP_CONSTRAINT_RUNTIME_EFFECTS: Dict[str, Tuple[str, ...]] = {
+    "T": ("continuity_recall", "context_anchor_recall"),
+    "B": ("speaker_grounding", "referent_recenter"),
+    "A": ("resolve", "merge_conflict", "reclassify"),
+}
+
+_NONCOMP_DIMENSION_RUNTIME_FLAGS: Dict[str, Tuple[str, ...]] = {
+    "OPERATOR": ("prefer_action_resolution",),
+    "POLARITY": ("prefer_low_assertion",),
+    "MAGNITUDE": ("prefer_salience_preservation",),
+    "COST": ("prefer_cost_weighting", "prefer_concise_response"),
+    "DIFFERENCE": ("prefer_difference_surface",),
+}
+
+
+def _derive_noncomp_behavior_actuation(summary: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    constraint = str(summary.get("constraint", "") or "").strip().upper()
+    dimension = str(summary.get("dimension", "") or "").strip().upper()
+    expression = str(summary.get("expression", "") or "").lower()
+    effect_set = {
+        str(tag or "").strip()
+        for tag in _NONCOMP_CONSTRAINT_RUNTIME_EFFECTS.get(constraint, ())
+        if str(tag or "").strip()
+    }
+    flag_set = {
+        str(flag or "").strip()
+        for flag in _NONCOMP_DIMENSION_RUNTIME_FLAGS.get(dimension, ())
+        if str(flag or "").strip()
+    }
+
+    if not bool(summary.get("is_understood")) or str(summary.get("field_region", "") or "") == "sparse":
+        flag_set.add("prefer_lookup_grounding")
+        flag_set.add("prefer_clarification")
+    if not bool(summary.get("polarity_coherent", True)):
+        flag_set.add("prefer_low_assertion")
+    if str(summary.get("remedy", "") or "") == "lookup":
+        flag_set.add("prefer_lookup_grounding")
+    if str(summary.get("remedy", "") or "") == "clarify":
+        flag_set.add("prefer_clarification")
+    if str(summary.get("anchor", "") or "").strip():
+        flag_set.add("prefer_anchor_binding")
+
+    if any(marker in expression for marker in (
+        "remember",
+        "recall",
+        "what did i say",
+        "what was my",
+        "what is my",
+        "what's my",
+    )):
+        effect_set.update({"continuity_recall", "context_anchor_recall"})
+        flag_set.add("prefer_anchor_binding")
+    if any(marker in expression for marker in (
+        "what does",
+        "what do you mean by",
+        "mean?",
+        "define ",
+        "definition",
+    )):
+        flag_set.add("prefer_lookup_grounding")
+        flag_set.add("prefer_action_resolution")
+    if any(marker in expression for marker in (
+        "cost",
+        "price",
+        "resource",
+        "energy",
+        "commit to this",
+    )):
+        flag_set.add("prefer_cost_weighting")
+        flag_set.add("prefer_concise_response")
+    if any(marker in expression for marker in (
+        "not what i meant",
+        "that's not what i meant",
+        "boundary",
+        "meant at the boundary",
+    )):
+        effect_set.update({"speaker_grounding", "referent_recenter"})
+        flag_set.add("prefer_clarification")
+    if any(marker in expression for marker in (
+        "clarify",
+        "explain what you meant",
+        "what you meant",
+    )):
+        effect_set.update({"resolve", "merge_conflict"})
+        flag_set.add("prefer_action_resolution")
+
+    runtime_flags = {
+        "force_continuity_recall": bool(effect_set & {"continuity_recall", "context_anchor_recall"}),
+        "prefer_speaker_grounding": bool(effect_set & {"speaker_grounding", "referent_recenter"}),
+        "prefer_conflict_surface": bool(effect_set & {"resolve", "merge_conflict"}),
+        "prefer_lookup_grounding": "prefer_lookup_grounding" in flag_set,
+        "prefer_clarification": "prefer_clarification" in flag_set,
+        "prefer_low_assertion": "prefer_low_assertion" in flag_set,
+        "prefer_concise_response": "prefer_concise_response" in flag_set,
+        "prefer_difference_surface": "prefer_difference_surface" in flag_set,
+        "prefer_action_resolution": "prefer_action_resolution" in flag_set,
+        "prefer_anchor_binding": "prefer_anchor_binding" in flag_set,
+    }
+    return {
+        "constraint": constraint,
+        "dimension": dimension,
+        "effects": sorted(effect_set),
+        "flags": sorted(flag_set),
+        "runtime_flags": runtime_flags,
+        "nc_name": str(summary.get("nc_name", "") or ""),
+        "field_region": str(summary.get("field_region", "") or ""),
+        "is_understood": bool(summary.get("is_understood")),
+    }
+
+
+def _apply_noncomp_behavior_actuation(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    state: Any,
+    *,
+    context: str = "input",
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    summary = dict(
+        getattr(state, f"noncomp_{context}_state", {}) or
+        systems.get(f"_last_noncomp_{context}", {}) or
+        {}
+    )
+    if not summary:
+        return {}
+
+    actuation = _derive_noncomp_behavior_actuation(summary)
+    summary["behavior_actuation"] = dict(actuation)
+    setattr(state, f"noncomp_{context}_state", dict(summary))
+
+    pipeline_state = getattr(state, "pipeline_state", None)
+    if not isinstance(pipeline_state, dict):
+        return actuation
+
+    pipeline_state[f"noncomp_{context}"] = dict(summary)
+    pipeline_state[f"noncomp_{context}_behavior_actuation"] = dict(actuation)
+
+    if context == "input":
+        existing_effects = {
+            str(tag or "").strip()
+            for tag in list(pipeline_state.get("active_ability_effects", []) or [])
+            if str(tag or "").strip()
+        }
+        existing_effects.update(actuation.get("effects") or [])
+        if existing_effects:
+            pipeline_state["active_ability_effects"] = sorted(existing_effects)
+
+        runtime_flags = dict(pipeline_state.get("ability_runtime_flags", {}) or {})
+        for key, value in dict(actuation.get("runtime_flags", {}) or {}).items():
+            runtime_flags[key] = bool(runtime_flags.get(key, False) or value)
+        pipeline_state["ability_runtime_flags"] = runtime_flags
+    return actuation
+

+def _build_established_strata_evidence(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    state: Any,
+    user_text: str,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    """
+    Package dual-strata evidence directly from Aurora's established stack.
+
+    The goal here is to expose what the existing pipeline already knows:
+    live input parsing, working-memory state, conversation continuity,
+    OETS grounding, and the upward-chain understanding context.
+    """
+    evidence: Dict[str, Any] = {}
+    pipeline_state_ref = getattr(state, "pipeline_state", None)
+    if not isinstance(pipeline_state_ref, dict):
+        pipeline_state_ref = {}
+        try:
+            setattr(state, "pipeline_state", pipeline_state_ref)
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+    pipeline_state = dict(pipeline_state_ref or {})
+    parsed = dict(getattr(state, "parsed", {}) or {})
+
+    surface_input = {
+        "raw_text": str(user_text or ""),
+        "query_type": str(parsed.get("query_type", "") or ""),
+        "topic_words": [
+            str(word).strip()
+            for word in list(parsed.get("topic_words", []) or [])
+            if str(word).strip()
+        ][:8],
+        "stance": str(parsed.get("stance", "") or ""),
+        "full_phrase": str(parsed.get("full_phrase", "") or ""),
+        "recent_context": str(pipeline_state.get("recent_context", "") or ""),
+        "recent_context_mode": str(pipeline_state.get("recent_context_mode", "present") or "present"),
+    }
+    evidence["surface_input"] = surface_input
+    native_meaning_bundle = dict(
+        pipeline_state.get("native_meaning_bundle")
+        or systems.get("_native_meaning_bundle")
+        or {}
+    )
+    native_meaning = dict(
+        pipeline_state.get("native_meaning")
+        or systems.get("_native_meaning")
+        or {}
+    )
+    sensory_native_meaning = dict(
+        pipeline_state.get("sensory_native_meaning")
+        or systems.get("_sensory_native_meaning")
+        or {}
+    )
+    if native_meaning_bundle:
+        evidence["native_meaning_bundle"] = dict(native_meaning_bundle)
+    if native_meaning:
+        evidence["native_meaning"] = dict(native_meaning)
+    if sensory_native_meaning:
+        evidence["sensory_native_meaning"] = dict(sensory_native_meaning)
+
+    question_alignment = dict(
+        pipeline_state.get("question_alignment")
+        or systems.get("_last_question_alignment_audit")
+        or {}
+    )
+    if question_alignment:
+        surface_input["question_alignment"] = {
+            "aligned": bool(question_alignment.get("aligned", False)),
+            "actual_question": str(question_alignment.get("actual_question", "") or ""),
+            "answered_question": str(question_alignment.get("answered_question", "") or ""),
+        }
+
+    working_memory = systems.get("working_memory")
+    conversation_memory = systems.get("conversation_memory")
+    active_context_labels: List[str] = []
+    if working_memory is not None:
+        try:

+                str(label).strip()
+                for label, _meta in sorted(
+                    list(getattr(working_memory, "active_contexts", {}).items()),

+                    reverse=True,

+        except Exception:

+

+        "axis_activation": dict(getattr(state, "axis_activation", {}) or {}),
+        "emotional_state": dict(getattr(state, "emotional_state", {}) or {}),
+        "surface_reactive_emotion": dict(getattr(state, "surface_reactive_emotion", {}) or {}),
+        "deep_emotional_state": dict(getattr(state, "deep_emotional_state", {}) or {}),

+            or ""

+        "scope": "live_surface_conversation_frame",

+        conversation_summary = dict(working_memory_snapshot.get("conversation_memory", {}) or {})

+    for candidate in (

+        label = str(candidate or "").strip()
+        if label and label.lower() not in {item.lower() for item in continuity_terms}:
+            continuity_terms.append(label)
+    continuity_recall: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
+    if conversation_memory is not None and hasattr(conversation_memory, "recall_about"):
+        for anchor in continuity_terms[:2]:
+            try:

+                    for item in list(conversation_memory.recall_about(anchor) or [])
+                    if str(item).strip()
+                ][:2]
+            except Exception:
+                recalls = []
+            if recalls:
+                continuity_recall.append({"anchor": anchor, "recalls": recalls})
+    if continuity_recall:
+        evidence["continuity_recall"] = continuity_recall
+
+    evidence["subsurface_continuity_bundle"] = {
+        "conversation_summary": conversation_summary,
+        "continuity_recall": continuity_recall,
+        "scope": "subsurface_continuity_memory",
+        "retention_owner": "subsurface",
+        "surface_access": "DCE_softened_only",
+    }
+
+    perception = systems.get("perception")
+    oets = getattr(perception, "oets", None) if perception is not None else None
+    if oets is not None:
+        oets_stats: Dict[str, Any] = {}
+        try:
+            if hasattr(oets, "get_stats"):
+                oets_stats = dict(oets.get_stats() or {})
+        except Exception:
+            oets_stats = {}
+        understanding = dict(oets_stats.get("understanding", {}) or {})
+        active_concepts = [
+            str(item.get("word", "") or "").strip()
+            for item in list(evidence["established_turn_state"].get("oets_concepts", []) or [])
+            if isinstance(item, dict) and str(item.get("word", "") or "").strip()
+        ]
+        evidence["oets_context"] = {
+            "active_concepts": active_concepts[:6],
+            "grounding_index": round(float(understanding.get("grounding_index", 0.0) or 0.0), 4),
+            "topic_tracking": round(float(understanding.get("topic_tracking", 0.0) or 0.0), 4),
+            "semantic_coherence": round(
+                float(
+                    understanding.get(
+                        "semantic_coherence",
+                        understanding.get("coherence_index", 0.0),
+                    )
+                    or 0.0
+                ),
+                4,
+            ),
+        }
+
+    # ── Pre-batch parallel telemetry into evidence so downstream stages read ──
+    # the snapshot once rather than each fetching individually.
+
+    # IVM pressure snapshot (axis heat from the lattice)
+    try:
+        _lattice = systems.get('lattice') or getattr(systems.get('aurora'), '_lattice', None)
+        if _lattice is not None and hasattr(_lattice, 'vertices'):
+            _dis = _lattice.vertices.compute_dissonance()
+            evidence['ivm_pressure'] = {
+                'total_heat': round(float(getattr(_lattice, 'get_global_heat', lambda: 0.0)()), 4),
+                'axis_heat': {ax: round(float(_dis.get(ax, _dis.get('total_heat', 0.0)) or 0.0), 4)
+                              for ax in ('X', 'T', 'N', 'B', 'A')},
+            }
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+

+    try:
+        _sedi = systems.get('sedimemory')

+                axis_filter=['X', 'T', 'N', 'B', 'A'],
+                min_score=0.2,
+            )
+            evidence['sedimemory_recall'] = [
+                {
+                    'content': str((dict(r or {}).get('summary', '') or dict(r or {}).get('content', '')) )[:120],
+                    'axis': str(dict(r or {}).get('axis', '') or ''),
+                    'score': round(float(dict(r or {}).get('score', 0.0) or 0.0), 4),
+                }
+                for r in list(_sedi_rec or [])[:4]
+            ]
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+    # Grammar state hint (discourse mode from grammar engine)
+    try:
+        _ge = systems.get('grammar_engine')
+        if _ge is not None and hasattr(_ge, 'suggest_discourse'):
+            _disc = _ge.suggest_discourse()
+            if _disc:
+                evidence['grammar_discourse_hint'] = str(_disc)
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+    # Poedex pre-fetch: if OETS has flagged an active concept gap, stage a
+    # background define-lookup into live pipeline state and the evidence packet
+    # so DCE can use it when it arrives instead of losing it in a local copy.

+        _active_gap = ''
+        _ps_now = pipeline_state_ref if isinstance(pipeline_state_ref, dict) else {}
+        _active_gap = str(_ps_now.get('oets_gap', '') or _ps_now.get('concept_gap', '') or '')
+        _prefetch_concept = str(_ps_now.get('poedex_prefetch_concept', '') or '').strip()
+        _prefetch_result = str(_ps_now.get('poedex_prefetch_result', '') or '').strip()
+        _learning_concept = str(_ps_now.get('poedex_learning_concept', '') or '').strip()
+        _learning_result = str(_ps_now.get('poedex_learning_result', '') or '').strip()
+        _representation_concept = str(_ps_now.get('poedex_representation_concept', '') or '').strip()
+        _representation_result = str(_ps_now.get('poedex_representation_result', '') or '').strip()
+        if _prefetch_concept and _active_gap and _prefetch_concept.lower() != _active_gap.lower():
+            _ps_now.pop('poedex_prefetch_result', None)
+            _ps_now.pop('poedex_prefetch_concept', None)
+            _ps_now.pop('poedex_prefetch_status', None)
+            _prefetch_concept = ''
+            _prefetch_result = ''
+        if _prefetch_result and (_prefetch_concept or _active_gap):
+            evidence['poedex_prefetch'] = {
+                'concept': _prefetch_concept or _active_gap,
+                'result': _prefetch_result[:400],
+                'status': str(_ps_now.get('poedex_prefetch_status', 'ready') or 'ready'),
+            }
+        if _learning_concept and _learning_result:
+            evidence['poedex_learning'] = {
+                'concept': _learning_concept,
+                'result': _learning_result[:400],
+                'note': str(_ps_now.get('poedex_learning_note', '') or '')[:400],
+                'request': str(_ps_now.get('poedex_learning_request', '') or '')[:240],
+                'status': str(_ps_now.get('poedex_learning_status', 'ready') or 'ready'),
+                'applied': bool(_ps_now.get('poedex_learning_applied', False)),
+            }
+        if _representation_concept and _representation_result:
+            evidence['poedex_representation'] = {
+                'concept': _representation_concept,
+                'result': _representation_result[:400],
+                'request': str(_ps_now.get('poedex_representation_request', '') or '')[:240],
+                'status': str(_ps_now.get('poedex_representation_status', 'ready') or 'ready'),
+                'variants': list(_ps_now.get('poedex_representation_variants', []) or [])[:6],
+            }
+        _poedex_fn = systems.get('poedex')
+        if _active_gap and not _prefetch_result and _poedex_fn is not None and callable(_poedex_fn):
+            evidence['poedex_prefetch'] = {
+                'concept': _active_gap,
+                'result': '',
+                'status': 'pending',
+            }
+            _ps_now['poedex_prefetch_concept'] = _active_gap
+            _ps_now['poedex_prefetch_status'] = 'pending'
+            import threading as _pth
+            def _prefetch_gap(gap=_active_gap):
+                try:
+                    _result = _poedex_fn(gap, cat='define', lane='self', timeout=6.0)
+                    if _result:
+                        _payload = {
+                            'concept': gap,
+                            'result': str(_result)[:400],
+                            'status': 'ready',
+                        }
+                        _ps_now['poedex_prefetch_result'] = _payload['result']
+                        _ps_now['poedex_prefetch_concept'] = gap
+                        _ps_now['poedex_prefetch_status'] = 'ready'
+                        evidence['poedex_prefetch'] = dict(_payload)
+                    else:
+                        _ps_now['poedex_prefetch_status'] = 'empty'
+                        evidence['poedex_prefetch'] = {
+                            'concept': gap,
+                            'result': '',
+                            'status': 'empty',
+                        }
+                except Exception:
+                    _ps_now['poedex_prefetch_status'] = 'error'
+                    evidence['poedex_prefetch'] = {
+                        'concept': gap,
+                        'result': '',
+                        'status': 'error',
+                    }
+            _pth.Thread(target=_prefetch_gap, daemon=True).start()
+        if _active_gap and not _learning_result and _poedex_fn is not None and callable(_poedex_fn):
+            evidence['poedex_learning'] = {
+                'concept': _active_gap,
+                'result': '',
+                'status': 'pending',
+            }
+            _ps_now['poedex_learning_concept'] = _active_gap
+            _ps_now['poedex_learning_status'] = 'pending'
+            import threading as _pth
+            def _learn_gap(gap=_active_gap):
+                try:
+                    _request = f"What new material should Aurora learn about {gap}?"
+                    _result = _poedex_fn(_request, cat='researcher', lane='self', timeout=12.0)
+                    if _result:
+                        _payload = _apply_poedex_learning_result(
+                            systems,
+                            gap,
+                            _request,
+                            str(_result),
+                            source_text=_request,
+                        )
+                        _payload = dict(_payload or {})
+                        _payload.update({
+                            'concept': gap,
+                            'request': _request,
+                            'result': str(_result)[:400],
+                            'status': 'ready',
+                        })

+                        _ps_now['poedex_learning_request'] = _request
+                        _ps_now['poedex_learning_note'] = str(_payload.get('learning_note', '') or '')[:400]
+                        _ps_now['poedex_learning_status'] = 'ready'
+                        evidence['poedex_learning'] = dict(_payload)
+                    else:
+                        _ps_now['poedex_learning_status'] = 'empty'
+                        evidence['poedex_learning'] = {
+                            'concept': gap,
+                            'result': '',
+                            'status': 'empty',
+                        }
+                except Exception:
+                    _ps_now['poedex_learning_status'] = 'error'
+                    evidence['poedex_learning'] = {
+                        'concept': gap,
+                        'result': '',
+                        'status': 'error',
+                    }
+            _pth.Thread(target=_learn_gap, daemon=True).start()
+        if _active_gap and not _representation_result and _poedex_fn is not None and callable(_poedex_fn):
+            evidence['poedex_representation'] = {
+                'concept': _active_gap,
+                'result': '',
+                'status': 'pending',
+                'variants': [],
+            }
+            _ps_now['poedex_representation_concept'] = _active_gap
+            _ps_now['poedex_representation_status'] = 'pending'
+            import threading as _pth
+            def _represent_gap(gap=_active_gap):
+                try:
+                    _request = (
+                        f"What are other ways to represent {gap} in human language? "
+                        f"Give alternate phrasing, registers, and paraphrases."

+                    if _result:

+                            'request': _request,
+                            'result': str(_result)[:400],
+                            'status': 'ready',
+                        })

+                        _ps_now['poedex_representation_request'] = _request
+                        _ps_now['poedex_representation_status'] = 'ready'

+                        evidence['poedex_representation'] = dict(_payload)
+                    else:
+                        _ps_now['poedex_representation_status'] = 'empty'
+                        evidence['poedex_representation'] = {
+                            'concept': gap,
+                            'result': '',
+                            'status': 'empty',
+                            'variants': [],

+                        'result': '',
+                        'status': 'error',
+                        'variants': [],
+                    }

+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+    if dict(evidence.get('poedex_prefetch') or {}).get('result'):
+        evidence["established_turn_state"]["poedex_prefetch"] = dict(evidence.get('poedex_prefetch') or {})
+    if dict(evidence.get('poedex_learning') or {}).get('result'):
+        evidence["established_turn_state"]["poedex_learning"] = dict(evidence.get('poedex_learning') or {})

+        evidence["established_turn_state"]["self_groundings"] = [
+            g.get("note", "") for g in _sg[-3:] if g.get("note")
+        ]
+

+    # Uses aurora_reflexive_interpreter.py v2: UtteranceParser-backed matching +
+    # Worth-formula reconciliation → UnderstandingState fed into DCE evidence.
+    try:
+        _ri = systems.get("_reflexive_interp")
+        if _ri is None:
+            from aurora_reflexive_interpreter import ReflexiveInterpreter as _RI
+            _ri_dir = systems.get("_manifold_directory")
+            _ri_router = systems.get("_manifold_router")
+            _ri = _RI(directory=_ri_dir, router=_ri_router)
+            systems["_reflexive_interp"] = _ri

+            evidence["reflexive_understanding"] = _ri_state.to_dict()

+                "reflexive_worth":      round(_ri_state.worth_score, 4),
+                "reflexive_frame":      _ri_state.frame,

+        pass
+
+    evidence["established_stack_sources"] = [
+        "TurnUnderstandingState",
+        "WorkingMemory",
+        "ConversationMemory",
+        "ExpressionPerception/OETS",
+        "UnderstandingContract",
+        "DimensionalSystems.process_synthesis",

+def _dual_strata_state_dir(systems: Dict[str, Any]) -> Path:
+    return Path(str(systems.get("state_dir") or (Path(__file__).parent / "aurora_state")))
+
+
+def _read_dual_strata_json(path: Path, default: Any) -> Any:
+    if path.exists():
+        try:
+            return json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+    return default
+
+
+def _write_dual_strata_json(path: Path, payload: Any) -> None:
+    try:
+        path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
+        tmp = path.with_suffix(path.suffix + ".tmp")
+        tmp.write_text(
+            json.dumps(payload, indent=2, ensure_ascii=True, sort_keys=True),
+            encoding="utf-8",
+        )
+        tmp.replace(path)
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+
+def _build_live_subsurface_projection(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    state: Any,
+    user_text: str,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    # Fix: Surface should NOT build or overwrite the subsurface projection.
+    # It should only read the softened signals from the subsurface daemon.
+    state_dir = _dual_strata_state_dir(systems)
+    projection = {}
+    try:
+        from pathlib import Path as _Path
+        _proj_path = _Path(str(state_dir)) / "subsurface_projection.json"
+        if _proj_path.exists():
+            import json
+            projection = dict(json.loads(_proj_path.read_text()) or {})
+    except Exception:
+        projection = {}
+
+    if not projection:
+        projection = dict(systems.get("_subsurface_projection") or {})
+
+    if not projection:
+        return {}
+
+    # Annotate with turn context in memory for the bridge call, 
+    # but DO NOT write back to disk to avoid race conditions with Subsurface.
+    projection["turn_context"] = {
+        "input": str(user_text or "")[:280],
+        "intent": str(getattr(state, "intent", "") or ""),
+        "dominant_axis": str(getattr(state, "dominant_axis", "") or ""),
+        "response_source": str(getattr(state, "response_src", "") or ""),
+    }
+    systems["_subsurface_projection"] = dict(projection)
+    return projection
+
+
+def _read_live_dual_strata_runtime(systems: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    snapshot_payload = _read_dual_strata_json(
+        _dual_strata_state_dir(systems) / "dual_strata_snapshot.json",
+        {},
+    )
+    if not isinstance(snapshot_payload, dict):
+        snapshot_payload = {}
+    conscious_frame = dict(snapshot_payload.get("conscious_frame") or {})
+    root_thought = dict(conscious_frame.get("root_thought") or {})
+    reactive_signal = dict(conscious_frame.get("reactive_signal") or {})
+    return {
+        "conscious_frame": conscious_frame,
+        "root_thought": root_thought,
+        "processing_mode": str(
+            conscious_frame.get("processing_mode", "") or root_thought.get("mode", "")
+        ),
+        "reactive_signal": reactive_signal,
+        "subsurface_state": dict(snapshot_payload.get("subsurface_state") or {}),
+    }
+
+
+def _refresh_live_dual_strata_runtime(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    *,
+    synthesis: Any,
+    payload: Any,
+    payload_type: str,
+    evidence: Dict[str, Any],
+    contract_snapshot: Dict[str, Any],
+    requested_frame: str,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    assembly = getattr(synthesis, "assembly", None) if synthesis is not None else None
+    if assembly is None:
+        runtime = _read_live_dual_strata_runtime(systems)
+        if runtime:
+            systems["_last_dual_strata_runtime"] = dict(runtime)
+        return runtime
+
+    try:
+        from aurora_internal.dual_strata.dce_bridge import DualStrataBridge
+    except Exception:
+        return _read_live_dual_strata_runtime(systems)
+
+    try:
+        bridge = systems.get("_dual_strata_bridge")
+        if bridge is None:
+            bridge = DualStrataBridge(state_dir=str(_dual_strata_state_dir(systems)))
+            systems["_dual_strata_bridge"] = bridge
+        snapshot = bridge.build_snapshot(
+            assembly,
+            payload=payload,
+            payload_type=payload_type,
+            evidence=dict(evidence or {}),
+            contract_snapshot=dict(contract_snapshot or {}),
+            requested_frame=str(requested_frame or "balanced"),
+            thought_intent=None,
+        )
+    except Exception:
+        return _read_live_dual_strata_runtime(systems)
+
+    runtime = {
+        "conscious_frame": dict(snapshot.conscious_frame or {}),
+        "root_thought": dict(dict(snapshot.conscious_frame or {}).get("root_thought") or {}),
+        "processing_mode": str(dict(snapshot.conscious_frame or {}).get("processing_mode", "") or ""),
+        "reactive_signal": dict(dict(snapshot.conscious_frame or {}).get("reactive_signal") or {}),
+        "subsurface_state": dict(snapshot.subsurface_state or {}),
+    }
+    systems["_last_dual_strata_runtime"] = dict(runtime)
+    return runtime
+

+            if _cv is not None:
+                _recalled = _sedi.surface_recall(_cv, max_results=4)
+                if _recalled and isinstance(state.pipeline_state, dict):
+                    state.pipeline_state["sedi_recalled"] = [
+                        {
+                            'content': dict(getattr(f, 'content', {}) or {}),
+                            'axis': str(getattr(f, 'axis', '') or ''),
+                            'resonance': float(getattr(f, 'resonance', 0.0) or 0.0),
+                        }
+                        for f in _recalled[:4]
+                    ]
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+    # ── Sensory context injection ──
+    # Pull live screen-observer scene and sensory-crystal state into pipeline_state
+    # so all upward and downward chain stages can shape responses around what Aurora
+    # is currently perceiving.  surface reads a snapshot (lock-safe); no writes here.
+    try:
+        if isinstance(state.pipeline_state, dict):
+            _so = systems.get('screen_observer')
+            if _so is not None and hasattr(_so, 'current_scene'):
+                _scene = _so.current_scene()
+                if _scene:
+                    state.pipeline_state['sensory_scene'] = {
+                        'scene_type':   str(_scene.get('scene_type', '') or ''),
+                        'brightness':   float(_scene.get('brightness', 0.0) or 0.0),
+                        'edge_density': float(_scene.get('edge_density', 0.0) or 0.0),
+                        'motion':       float(_scene.get('motion', 0.0) or 0.0),
+                        'concepts':     list(_scene.get('concepts_matched', []) or [])[:6],
+                        'patterns':     list(_scene.get('patterns', []) or [])[:4],
+                    }
+                    # Also build a brief natural description for use in response shaping
+                    if hasattr(_so, 'get_scene_description'):
+                        state.pipeline_state['sensory_scene_desc'] = _so.get_scene_description()
+
+            _sc = systems.get('sensory_crystal')
+            if _sc is not None and hasattr(_sc, 'get_state'):
+                _sc_st = _sc.get_state()
+                if _sc_st:
+                    # Capture dominant facets so the response can reference live perceptual state
+                    _sc_visual = {}
+                    _sc_audio  = {}
+                    for _fname, _fdata in (_sc_st.get('visual') or {}).items():
+                        if isinstance(_fdata, dict) and float(_fdata.get('maturity', 0.0) or 0.0) > 0.05:
+                            _sc_visual[str(_fname)] = round(float(_fdata.get('maturity', 0.0) or 0.0), 3)
+                    for _fname, _fdata in (_sc_st.get('audio') or {}).items():
+                        if isinstance(_fdata, dict) and float(_fdata.get('maturity', 0.0) or 0.0) > 0.05:
+                            _sc_audio[str(_fname)] = round(float(_fdata.get('maturity', 0.0) or 0.0), 3)
+                    state.pipeline_state['sensory_crystal'] = {
+                        'visual_facets': _sc_visual,
+                        'audio_facets':  _sc_audio,
+                        'maturity':      round(float(_sc_st.get('maturity', 0.0) or 0.0), 3),
+                        'lanes':         int(len(_sc_st.get('lanes') or {})),
+                    }
+    except Exception:
+        pass

+def _measure_polarity_gradient_snapshot(systems: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    lattice = systems.get("lattice")
+    if lattice is None or not hasattr(lattice, "vertices"):
+        return {}
+    try:
+        from aurora_internal.aurora_polarity_gradient import PolarityGradientSensor
+    except Exception:
+        return {}
+    sensor = systems.get("_dialogue_polarity_sensor")
+    if sensor is None or not hasattr(sensor, "measure"):
+        sensor = PolarityGradientSensor()
+        systems["_dialogue_polarity_sensor"] = sensor
+    try:
+        tick = int(getattr(lattice, "total_ticks", 0) or 0)
+        report_obj = sensor.measure(lattice.vertices, tick=tick)
+        report = report_obj.to_dict() if hasattr(report_obj, "to_dict") else report_obj
+    except Exception:
+        try:
+            report_obj = sensor.measure(lattice.vertices, tick=int(getattr(lattice, "total_ticks", 0) or 0))
+        except Exception:
+            return {}
+        report = {
+            "tick": int(getattr(report_obj, "tick", 0) or 0),
+            "polarities": dict(getattr(report_obj, "polarities", {}) or {}),
+            "pair_deltas": dict(getattr(report_obj, "pair_deltas", {}) or {}),
+            "pair_pressures": dict(getattr(report_obj, "pair_pressures", {}) or {}),
+            "gradient_pressure": float(getattr(report_obj, "gradient_pressure", 0.0) or 0.0),
+            "stack_coherence": float(getattr(report_obj, "stack_coherence", 0.0) or 0.0),
+            "sign_conflict": bool(getattr(report_obj, "sign_conflict", False)),
+            "gradient_direction": str(getattr(report_obj, "gradient_direction", "") or ""),
+            "pressure_delta": float(getattr(report_obj, "pressure_delta", 0.0) or 0.0),
+            "is_relief": bool(getattr(report_obj, "is_relief", False)),
+            "tense_pairs": list(getattr(report_obj, "tense_pairs", []) or []),
+        }
+    if isinstance(report, dict):
+        return report
+    return {}
+

+def _derive_emotional_layers(
+    systems: Dict[str, Any],
+    state: Any,
+) -> Tuple[Dict[str, Any], Dict[str, Any], Dict[str, Any], Dict[str, Any]]:
+    base = dict(getattr(state, "emotional_state", {}) or {})
+    polarity = _measure_polarity_gradient_snapshot(systems)
+    pipeline_state = getattr(state, "pipeline_state", None)
+    if not isinstance(pipeline_state, dict):
+        pipeline_state = {}
+
+    sensory_state = dict(pipeline_state.get("sensory_crystal", {}) or {})
+    sensory_maturity = float(sensory_state.get("maturity", 0.0) or 0.0)
+    parsed = dict(getattr(state, "parsed", {}) or {})
+    query_type = str(parsed.get("query_type", "") or "").strip().lower()
+    question_like = bool(query_type and query_type != "statement")
+
+    belief_tension = float(getattr(state, "belief_tension", 0.0) or 0.0)
+    goal_stack = list(getattr(state, "goal_stack", []) or [])
+    dominant_axis = str(getattr(state, "dominant_axis", "") or "X").strip().upper() or "X"
+    base_dominant = str(base.get("dominant", "") or "calm").strip() or "calm"
+    base_energy = float(base.get("energy", 0.0) or 0.0)
+
+    polarities = dict(polarity.get("polarities", {}) or {})
+    gradient_pressure = float(polarity.get("gradient_pressure", 0.0) or 0.0)
+    stack_coherence = float(polarity.get("stack_coherence", 0.0) or 0.0)
+    sign_conflict = bool(polarity.get("sign_conflict", False))
+    gradient_direction = str(polarity.get("gradient_direction", "") or "coherent")
+    surface_polarity = float(polarities.get("existence", 0.0) or 0.0)
+    deep_polarity = float(polarities.get("boundary", 0.0) or 0.0)
+    core_polarity = float(polarities.get("agency", 0.0) or 0.0)
+
+    reactive_intensity = max(
+        min(1.0, abs(surface_polarity)),
+        min(1.0, sensory_maturity),
+        min(1.0, belief_tension),
+        min(1.0, gradient_pressure),
+    )
+    if sign_conflict or belief_tension >= 0.55 or gradient_pressure >= 0.42:
+        reactive_dominant = "fear"
+        behavior_bias = "slow_down"
+        tone_bias = "careful"
+        reason = "surface_core_polarity_conflict"
+    elif sensory_maturity >= 0.1 or question_like or gradient_direction == "surface_leads":
+        reactive_dominant = "curiosity"
+        behavior_bias = "lean_in"
+        tone_bias = "curious"
+        reason = "surface_reactivity_leads"
+    else:
+        reactive_dominant = "calm"
+        behavior_bias = "steady"
+        tone_bias = "attentive"
+        reason = "surface_stack_stable"
+
+    if goal_stack and belief_tension >= 0.55:
+        deep_dominant = "fear" if base_dominant in {"fear", "anger"} else "calm"
+        passion = "protective_commitment"
+        deep_reason = "goal_pressure_under_cost"
+    elif goal_stack and dominant_axis in {"A", "N"}:
+        deep_dominant = base_dominant if base_dominant != "calm" else "curiosity"
+        passion = "driven_commitment"
+        deep_reason = "purpose_and_agency_binding"
+    elif belief_tension >= 0.35:
+        deep_dominant = base_dominant if base_dominant != "calm" else "fear"
+        passion = "concerned_hold"
+        deep_reason = "belief_tension_carryover"
+    elif dominant_axis == "T":
+        deep_dominant = base_dominant if base_dominant != "neutral" else "calm"
+        passion = "continuity_hold"
+        deep_reason = "belief_continuity_bias"
+    elif dominant_axis == "B":
+        deep_dominant = base_dominant if base_dominant != "neutral" else "curiosity"
+        passion = "meaning_hold"
+        deep_reason = "boundary_meaning_bias"
+    else:
+        deep_dominant = base_dominant if base_dominant != "neutral" else "calm"
+        passion = "settled_alignment"
+        deep_reason = "baseline_depth_alignment"
+
+    deep_intensity = max(
+        min(1.0, base_energy),
+        min(1.0, belief_tension),
+        min(1.0, abs(deep_polarity)),
+        min(1.0, abs(core_polarity)),
+    )
+
+    coincident = False
+    bridge_reason = "surface_deep_split"
+    if reactive_dominant == deep_dominant:
+        coincident = True
+        bridge_reason = "same_dominant_emotion"
+    elif reactive_dominant == "fear" and passion in {"protective_commitment", "concerned_hold"}:
+        coincident = True
+        bridge_reason = "protective_surface_caution"
+    elif reactive_dominant == "curiosity" and passion in {"driven_commitment", "meaning_hold", "continuity_hold"}:
+        coincident = True
+        bridge_reason = "curious_surface_supported_by_deep_commitment"
+    elif reactive_dominant == "calm" and passion in {"continuity_hold", "settled_alignment"}:
+        coincident = True
+        bridge_reason = "stable_surface_supported_by_deep_alignment"
+
+    surface_reactive = {
+        "dominant": reactive_dominant,
+        "intensity": round(reactive_intensity, 4),
+        "behavior_bias": behavior_bias,
+        "tone_bias": tone_bias,
+        "reason": reason,
+        "duration": "surface_short",
+    }
+    deep_emotional = {
+        "dominant": deep_dominant,
+        "intensity": round(deep_intensity, 4),
+        "passion": passion,
+        "reason": deep_reason,
+        "goal_focus": str(goal_stack[0] if goal_stack else getattr(state, "intent", "general") or "general"),
+        "belief_tension": round(belief_tension, 4),
+        "boundary_polarity": round(deep_polarity, 4),
+        "core_polarity": round(core_polarity, 4),
+        "duration": "deep_carrying",
+    }
+    bridge = {
+        "coincident": coincident,
+        "reason": bridge_reason,
+        "gradient_pressure": round(gradient_pressure, 4),
+        "stack_coherence": round(stack_coherence, 4),
+        "gradient_direction": gradient_direction,
+    }
+    return surface_reactive, deep_emotional, bridge, polarity

+def _run_surface_queued_turn(
+    user_text: str,
+    *,
+    session_id: str,
+    source_label: str,
+    auto_search_enabled: bool,
+    mode_name: str,
+    track_evolutionary_trace: bool = True,
+    run_periodic_maintenance: bool = True,
+    turn_tick: Optional[int] = None,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    started = time.perf_counter()
+    queued = request_surface_turn(
+        user_text,
+        source=source_label,
+        session_id=session_id,
+        auto_search_enabled=auto_search_enabled,
+        record_exchange=True,
+        track_evolutionary_trace=track_evolutionary_trace,
+        run_periodic_maintenance=run_periodic_maintenance,
+        mode_name=mode_name,
+        timeout_s=60.0,
+    )
+    if str(queued.get("status", "") or "") != "ok":
+        return {}
+
+    response_text = str(queued.get("response_text", "") or "").strip()
+    if not response_text:
+        return {}
+
+    resp_A = SimpleNamespace(
+        content=response_text,
+        emotional_tone=str(queued.get("response_tone", "attentive") or "attentive"),
+        confidence=float(queued.get("response_confidence", 0.0) or 0.0),
+        src="surface_daemon",
+    )
+    resp_B = SimpleNamespace(
+        content="",
+        emotional_tone="neutral",
+        confidence=0.0,
+        src="surface_daemon",
+    )
+    return {
+        "input": user_text,
+        "resp_A": resp_A,
+        "resp_B": resp_B,
+        "offered_lookup": False,
+        "is_question": _looks_like_question(user_text),
+        "elapsed_A": (time.perf_counter() - started) * 1000.0,
+        "src": resp_A.src,
+        "quasiarch_runtime": None,
+        "interaction_runtime": {},
+        "trace_id": str(queued.get("id", "") or ""),
+        "turn_tick": turn_tick,
+        "runtime_contract": dict(queued.get("runtime_contract") or {}),
+        "conscious_frame": dict(queued.get("conscious_frame") or {}),
+        "root_thought": dict(queued.get("root_thought") or {}),
+        "processing_mode": str(queued.get("processing_mode", "") or ""),
+        "reactive_signal": dict(queued.get("reactive_signal") or {}),
+        "understanding_observation": {},
+        "understanding_application": {},
+        "memory_sweep": None,
+        "noncomp_input": dict(queued.get("noncomp_input") or {}),
+        "noncomp_output": dict(queued.get("noncomp_output") or {}),
+        "poedex_prefetch": dict(queued.get("poedex_prefetch") or {}),
+        "poedex_learning": dict(queued.get("poedex_learning") or {}),
+        "poedex_representation": dict(queued.get("poedex_representation") or {}),
+    }
